Current Affairs Commentary

On "Frugality to Save the Nation" 10

— Dou

Recently, Chairman Lin of the National Government gave a speech on "Frugality to Save the Nation" at the Central Broadcasting Station, emphasizing the importance of the national economy, believing that the manifestation of national strength lies in this, so the construction of the national economy is indeed a matter of urgency. His argument on frugality is divided into four points: first, saving expenses; second, cherishing time; third, having a stable career; and fourth, promoting domestic goods. These are benevolent words that everyone should admire. At the same time, Premier Chiang Kai-shek of the Executive Yuan, when instructing the authorities of Guangdong Province and cities, earnestly spoke about reforming politics. In summary, there are also four points: first, diligent investigation to find talent; second, seeking speed and accuracy to revitalize; third, bearing grievances to achieve reform; and fourth, cooperation to ensure success. Although this may differ from Lin's point of view, there is no difference in their goals. Economic construction must rely on political power for promotion, and political construction must take the promotion of frugality as the first task. The two have common ground. The fact that the two major leaders in the central government have given such important reminders one after another is enough to inspire deep thought, and its contribution is not small. While we are happy to hear it, we still want to elaborate on it and dare to take this opportunity to comment on it.

The extravagant social atmosphere today is an undeniable fact. Chairman Lin's theory of "Frugality to Save the Nation" can be said to be a good medicine for the problem. However, if we want to change the atmosphere, we must start from the top and gradually promote it to the bottom in order to achieve effectiveness. Most of the people are trapped under the pressure of life, and frugality is not enough. How can they afford to be wasteful? Even those who are slightly better off and work hard to make a living may not be criticized for being excessive or decadent. The source of the decadent atmosphere lies in the fact that there are too many people with leisure. Because they have leisure, they do not "cherish time," and even take advantage of their special privileges to despise all restrictions, creating an unfathomable situation. As a result, those who "have a stable career" are unable to resist the temptations of material things or escape the push of the environment, and are unable to adhere to their own aspirations and follow suit. It is difficult to reverse the situation, which is regrettable. If those in power have a thorough understanding and can set an example and use the power of politics to implement gradual pressure, then there is still hope for improvement. Chiang's expectations for administrative personnel also coincide with the meaning of frugality. It is necessary to know that all administrative officials must first have a focused spirit in order to be quick to respond to opportunities. They must first have a unique integrity in order to be able to bear grievances without fail. If you want to form these two styles, what can you seek other than frugality? Only frugality can cut off the privatization of cliques, and only accuracy can save the mind from distractions. The ancient people said that frugality cultivates integrity, which is a timeless truth. Those in politics today should reflect on these words.

Japanese Foreign Minister Hosts Foreign Correspondents: Clarifies Japan's Attitude Towards China, Believes China Has Reached a Crossroads, Cannot Continue with Delaying Tactics, Hopes for a Friendly Path 11

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita hosted forty members of the foreign press corps stationed in Beijing at his official residence at 3 p.m. on the 28th, holding a tea party to clarify the Imperial Government's attitude towards the current state of Sino-Japanese relations. He also detailed the Imperial Government's view of the rampant anti-Japanese terrorism in China, and affirmed the unwavering peaceful policy of stabilizing the situation in East Asia. (28th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita issued the following statement when hosting foreign correspondents stationed in Beijing on the 28th: Japan's diplomatic policy was explained in detail to you gentlemen at the meeting on April 25th of this year. However, since my assumption of the post of Foreign Minister, with the aim of ensuring stability in East Asia, I first hoped for the adjustment of relations between China and Japan. Unfortunately, this attempt has not yielded any concrete results, causing various pending issues between the two countries to increase the somber atmosphere. On August 24th, two Japanese nationals in Chengdu were suddenly killed by violent thugs, and two others were seriously injured. While this matter was being negotiated in Nanjing, a number of unfortunate incidents occurred in Beihai, Shantou, Hankou, and Shanghai against Japanese soldiers, officials, and Japanese residents in China. The Chinese authorities have repeatedly issued statements and promised to suppress anti-Japanese activities, but looking back over the past ten months, the number of incidents in which Japanese citizens in China have been harmed by vicious means has been very frequent, with more than ten major incidents alone. As a result, the lives and property of many Japanese in China have been under serious threat and deep anxiety. These unfortunate incidents are of course attributable to the anti-Japanese education and anti-Japanese policies, such as incitement of anti-Japanese sentiment, by the National Government and the Kuomintang over the years. It is also possible that some of these incidents are due to what the Chinese side calls the Communist Party's attempts to sow discord between China and Japan. However, when resolving such unfortunate incidents, if the Chinese side only sees them as ordinary murder cases and seeks to resolve the situation, it is difficult to be satisfied and even more difficult to prevent the recurrence of such unfortunate incidents. It is imperative to trace the root cause and consider countermeasures. To ensure the future, the Chinese side should passively and diligently implement the suppression of anti-Japanese sentiment and anti-Japanese activities (as for the ineffectiveness of the edict on friendship, it can be proved by the current situation) and actively seek the adjustment of relations between the two countries to eradicate the roots of anti-Japanese sentiment and anti-Japanese activities. Furthermore, measures against the Communist Party must also be considered. The Imperial Government, based on the above principles, is seeking to resolve each of these individual problems and is currently negotiating with the Nanjing government on the issue of adjusting relations between the two countries. However, progress is slow, and in the meantime, new unfortunate incidents continue to occur elsewhere. The Japanese side earnestly hopes to resolve the situation peacefully through diplomatic negotiations so as to truly ensure the stability of East Asia. However, as you gentlemen know, the argument that negotiations are useless has long been prevalent among the domestic population and Japanese residents in China. However, even if negotiations are suspended, the lives and property of many Japanese in China cannot be left in a state of insecurity. Therefore, at that time, measures would have to be considered separately. As for the outcome of this negotiation, the relationship between China and Japan will either be very good or very bad. Therefore, we cannot continue with the ambiguous attitude of the past. Therefore, the Chinese side at this moment is standing at a major crossroads where it must choose to shake hands with Japan. However, I hope that China will overcome all difficulties and shake hands with Japan. (28th, Domei News Agency dispatch)

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita delivered a lengthy speech today, stating that his intention was to show the world Japan's attitude. Among other things, he said that China is now at a critical crossroads, and that no matter what difficulties China may have, it must overcome them. He earnestly hoped that China would shake hands with Japan and reciprocate with friendship. The outcome of the current Sino-Japanese negotiations will either improve relations between the two countries or worsen them. In the current situation, China is not allowed to delay matters with an ambiguous attitude as in the past. The Foreign Minister's strong remarks were unexpected, and were made when he received forty foreign reporters at the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. The main points of his statement and his answers to the reporters' questions are recorded below:

The Chinese government and the Kuomintang cannot shirk their responsibility for the recent anti-Japanese incidents in China. China should exercise more effective control over the anti-Japanese movement and make more constructive efforts to improve Sino-Japanese relations. For the sake of a permanent solution, the roots of anti-Japanese turmoil should be eradicated. Public opinion in Japan and Japanese residents in China are increasingly advocating that continuing negotiations with China are of no avail. If the current negotiations fail and end, the Japanese authorities cannot allow the lives and property of Japanese residents in China to continue to be in any danger, and it will be necessary to consider final countermeasures. Japan hopes that China will formulate a fixed and constructive program to eliminate anti-Japanese sentiment. At the beginning of his speech, Arita sincerely stated that since taking office (March 9, 1936), he has been diligently working to adjust Sino-Japanese relations. However, this effort has not yielded substantial results, and various problems remain unresolved, causing a haze that makes relations between the two countries increasingly bleak. Arita mentioned the cases of Shantou, Chengdu, Beihai, Hankou, and Shanghai, saying that the victims included Japanese soldiers, officials, and residents. Although the Chinese authorities have repeatedly issued announcements promising to curb the anti-Japanese movement, these have been empty promises. Japanese residents in China have been subjected to unspeakable acts of violence by anti-Japanese elements in China, so the lives and property of many Japanese residents in China are now under great threat, and they naturally feel deeply uneasy. All these unfortunate incidents can be said to be the natural result of the anti-Japanese education, anti-Japanese propaganda, anti-Japanese policies, and other forms of anti-Japanese activity that China has implemented for many years. This is a responsibility that the National Government and the Kuomintang cannot shirk. Merely resolving these few incidents is not enough. The Chinese authorities should take resolute steps to eradicate the root of the problem to prevent the recurrence of these incidents. For the sake of a permanent solution, China should strive to eradicate the turmoil of anti-Japanese sentiment. The Japanese government has been conducting negotiations with the Chinese government in this spirit to resolve various cases and adjust Sino-Japanese relations, but these negotiations have not made significant progress. At the same time, new incidents of a similar nature are sprouting up. The resolution between China and Japan should be achieved as far as possible through diplomatic negotiations by peaceful means, so that the security of East Asia can be truly guaranteed. This is Japan's sincere aspiration. Arita then answered many questions, saying that he sincerely hoped to achieve his aspiration through diplomatic negotiations. When asked if the failure of negotiations would mean war, Arita replied, "The word 'war' is not included in the diplomatic vocabulary." Arita continued to say that he sincerely hoped that China would respond to Japan's friendly attitude. For this reason, he sincerely hoped that China would draft a fixed program to eliminate anti-Japanese sentiment. Now that the Southwest problem has been resolved, President Chiang Kai-shek should urgently return to Nanjing to resolve the anti-Japanese cases and eliminate the root and deep-seated cause of the disaster, thereby bringing Sino-Japanese relations into clarity and making the two countries more friendly. He feared that the Chinese government still did not truly understand the seriousness of the overall situation, which could be discerned from the news reported in the newspapers and the mistakes made in Nanjing. (28th, Reuters dispatch)

Japan's Southern Advance Policy - The Army and Navy Request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs - To Negotiate with the Philippines and the Dutch East Indies 23

(Tokyo) According to sources here, the Japanese Army and Navy, and other provinces that pay attention to Japan's expansion into the South Pacific, have decided to request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to hold public negotiations with the Philippines and the Dutch East Indies, so that the two places will lift their restrictions on Japanese immigrants. It is reported that this decision is the result of repeated meetings and discussions by personnel from the Japanese Army and Navy, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, and the Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce. Their opinion is that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs seems to have overlooked the importance of Japan's southern expansion, so it should be requested to adopt a more forceful policy on this matter. Japan's gaze has long been focused on the above-mentioned places as outlets for its surplus population. The Ministry of Colonial Affairs, which is responsible for the immigration issue, is naturally the most concerned. However, without the cooperation of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the province cannot conduct negotiations with the Philippines and the Dutch East Indies. According to Article 3 of the United States Immigration Law of 1917, contract laborers are prohibited from entering the Philippines. In fact, only a small number of Japanese laborers are permitted to enter under the condition that they are only engaged in agriculture and commerce. As for the Dutch East Indies, there is a law on foreigners entering the country, which adopts a quota system for immigrants from various countries. Under this system, Japan immigrates about 800 people to the Dutch East Indies each year. According to statistics from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, as of November 1, 1933, the number of Japanese residents in the Philippines was 20,400, and the number of Japanese residents in the Dutch East Indies was only 6,900. (28th, Reuters dispatch)

Philippine Business - Overseas Chinese Business - Seized by the Japanese 24

(Washington) The United States Department of Commerce recently analyzed Philippine business and stated that Japanese residents in the Philippines have seized much of the small-scale business of overseas Chinese, resulting in a large increase in Japanese imports to the Philippines last year. In total, Japanese residents accounted for nearly 35 percent of the total retail sales in the Philippines last year. In 1933, Japanese stores accounted for only 25 percent, while Chinese stores accounted for 40 percent, which is in line with the ratio of 20 percent and 50 percent in 1932. The Japanese have spared no effort in promoting their goods, so Japanese goods accounted for 14.23% of the total imports to the Philippines last year. Most of the increase in Japanese goods was at the expense of American goods, with only a few exceptions. In recent years, the Japanese have been trying to get rid of their reliance on overseas Chinese to run retail businesses, and have set up import branches in various ports in the Philippines and encouraged Japanese residents to set up stores, giving them long-term credit. Japanese stores are mostly clean, and their goods are cheap and of good quality, so they have been very effective. Now there are Japanese stores in various cities and towns, competing with Chinese stores. (27th, National News Agency dispatch)

China's Antimony Production - Still Holds the World's Lead 25

(Washington) The United States Bureau of Mines published the 1936 Minerals Yearbook, which stated that the antimony industry in 1935 had progressed with the industrial recovery. China still holds the world's lead in antimony production, but Mexico, Bolivia, and Peru have also greatly increased their production, which has greatly increased their production, posing a threat to China's market. Last year, due to strong sales, antimony prices soared. The greatest need was in Europe, which was naturally due to arms manufacturing. In the United States, the demand for antimony also increased due to the increase in automobile production. China's antimony industry is still subject to government control, so as sales have increased, antimony prices have also risen. The antimony produced in the Americas is slightly cheaper. In total, the production of the world's major producing countries last year was 17,700 tons for China, 3,656 tons for Mexico, 2,674 tons for Bolivia, and 343 tons for Peru. In addition, the production of antimony in Africa has also increased in recent years, and the world's antimony ore reserves are still rich, so they will not be exhausted for a while. (27th, National News Agency dispatch)

Qiqihar - Russian Consulate Closed 26

Qiqihar - The Soviet Russian Consulate in Qiqihar was ordered by the government of its country to close on September 25. Consul Kresnikoff and other staff members are scheduled to go to Harbin on the day of Bingshen. (28th, Domei dispatch)

Chinese Tea Exports to the United States - Less Than Japan and Taiwan 27

(Washington) The United States Food and Drug Administration published its annual tea report, which stated that in the fiscal year ending June 30 of this year, black tea from the Dutch East Indies, India, and Ceylon has greatly increased in sales in the United States, while green tea from Japan and China has declined. The consumption of tea in the United States has not changed much in the past three years, at approximately 84 million pounds, but it has decreased significantly compared to the annual import of approximately 100 million pounds ten years ago. The green tea imported from Japan and China has continued to decrease, while black tea and oolong tea have increased slightly. The total amount of tea exported from China to the United States last year, including red, green, and oolong teas, was 6,128,142 pounds, accounting for only 7.3 percent of the total imports to the United States. Black tea accounted for the most. Tea from Japan and Taiwan accounted for 25.21 percent. Japan mainly exports green tea, Taiwan mainly exports oolong tea, but black tea has also increased. The proportion of tea exports from Japan and Taiwan to the United States has not changed much in the past five years. (27th, National News Agency dispatch)

Netherlands and Switzerland Announce Currency Devaluation, Greece and Latvia Also Join the Sterling Bloc 30

The Hague. Dutch Prime Minister Dr. Colijn delivered a radio address this morning, stating that after Switzerland adopted a currency devaluation policy, the Dutch government had no choice but to reconsider its traditional monetary policy. It has now ordered a ban on gold exports. In addition, an Exchange Equalisation Fund has been established to stabilize foreign exchange. In the future, the price of imported goods will inevitably rise, but the price of domestic goods will not necessarily increase accordingly. Citizens should not raise prices or hide gold. (Havas, 28th)

The Hague. Dutch Prime Minister Colijn announced in a radio broadcast in Amsterdam today that the Netherlands would also follow Britain in adopting a managed currency system, and asked the people to remain calm and have confidence in the government. The government is confident that it can work with the Dutch Bank to manage the value of the guilder. According to announcements here, both houses of the Dutch Parliament have convened emergency meetings. Colijn did not mention devaluation in his broadcast speech, but hinted that the value of the guilder might weaken slightly. Colijn also announced the establishment of a 300 million guilder equalisation fund and immediately introduced legislation to prevent rapid price increases. While Colijn did not specify how much the value of the guilder would be devalued in the future, banking circles informally indicated that the value of the guilder might be devalued by about 10%, the extent of which would depend on the progress of prices. The calmness of Colijn's speech gave the financial community a very good impression. Although the stock exchange was closed today, other markets were open as usual, but transactions were limited and only at nominal prices. (Reuters, 28th)

The Hague. Reliable sources say today that the Dutch government has decided to adopt the managed currency system implemented by the United Kingdom after abandoning the gold standard in order to devalue the Dutch guilder by 5 to 20 percent, and to allocate 150 million guilders to establish an equalisation fund to adjust exchange rate fluctuations. (Reuters, 28th)

Bern. The Swiss Federal Government has recently issued an order stipulating that the weight of pure gold contained in the Swiss franc be reduced to between 0.190 grams and 0.215 grams, which means a devaluation of 30%. (The original weight of pure gold contained in the Swiss franc was 0.29025 grams, so the devaluation rate is between 34.54% and 25.95%, with an average of 30%.) The Public Economy Department has also issued an order stipulating that domestic wholesale and retail prices, hotel expenses, gas, electricity, and rent, etc., may not be increased without the special permission of the department. (Havas, 27th)

Bern. Officials announced today that the gold content of the Swiss franc will be reduced to between 26% and 34.5%, equivalent to 21.4 to 24.17 US cents, compared to 32.67 cents previously. (National Telegram, 27th)

Athens. The government has decided to revalue the drachma (Greek currency) according to the British pound, and stipulates that from today, the buying and selling prices of the pound are as follows: buying at 546 drachmas per pound, selling at 550 drachmas per pound. (Havas, 28th)

Riga. The Latvian government has decided to revalue its currency, the lat, according to the average exchange rate against the British pound in 1931, that is, 25.22 lats per pound. (Havas, 28th)

Italy and Germany Consider New Monetary Situation, US Plans to Revise Gold Export Regulations, Turkey Maintains Status Quo 31

(Berlin) According to German Finance Minister Reinhardt today, Germany is not considering abandoning the gold standard. Financial circles are quite calm about the devaluation of the franc. (Reuters, 27th)

The authorities are quite anxious about the impact of the franc devaluation on travellers, because Italy's foreign exchange income largely depends on the tourism industry. (Reuters, 28th)

(Washington) The government and financial circles are currently discussing the possibility of the United States revising its strict regulations on cash exports to allow gold to circulate more freely among countries participating in international monetary agreements. It is felt that as a result of the establishment of this agreement, the United States' huge amount of gold may flow out slightly. According to current regulations on gold exports, gold can only be shipped to countries that still use the full gold standard, such as France, the Netherlands, and Switzerland. If the restoration of monetary balance between various economic systems is successful, it is believed that gold should be allowed to circulate among countries participating in international monetary agreements to facilitate the adjustment of international trade imbalances. Treasury Secretary Morgenthau met with President Roosevelt today, mainly to determine the Treasury Department's policy on gold exports. (Reuters, 27th)

Soviet Russia Denies Selling One Million Pounds 32

(Moscow) Local newspapers published a statement from the Soviet State Bank, saying that according to a report from the United Press in Washington, US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau made a statement to reporters on the 20th of this month, claiming that an agent of the Soviet State Bank had sold one million pounds of British currency in the financial market without limit, in an attempt to depress the price of the pound. Fortunately, he (Morgenthau) intervened and used American balance funds to purchase the pounds, so as to avoid the results of the Soviet State Bank's methods. The State Bank now declares that Morgenthau's statement, claiming that the Soviet State Bank intended to depress the pound, is completely unfounded slander. The pretext used by Morgenthau for his statement was ordinary banking business conducted by the State Bank through its agent, Chase Bank in New York. On October 1st of this year, the Soviet Union will, before the due date, use Stockholm's Enskilda Bank to redeem a batch of bonds issued in 1931 held by the well-known Swedish manufacturer ACEA, totaling US$6,890,700. The Soviet government had announced this matter in advance in newspapers in the Soviet Union and other countries in June of this year. In order to handle this business, the Soviet State Bank notified its permanent agent in New York, Chase Bank, on September 25th of this year to perform the following two procedures: (1) remit US$6,890,700 to Stockholm's Enskilda Bank; (2) sell one million pounds of British currency at the highest possible price (the State Bank had specifically pointed this out in a telegram to Chase Bank on September 25th), equivalent to US$5 million, to replenish the State Bank's US dollar account at Chase Bank. This is ordinary banking business, but US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau actually used it as a pretext for the Soviet Union to disrupt the world's financial balance and the pound's exchange rate, which is really strange. Therefore, Morgenthau's statement about the Soviet State Bank is obviously unfounded and gives people the impression of a non-noble anti-Soviet slander, the purpose of which is not to protect international monetary balance or the pound's exchange rate, but to serve other purposes. (TASS, 28th)

(Paris) It is reported that the Soviet Union sold one million pounds in the New York market yesterday, which was absorbed by the US Treasury Department. According to well-informed sources, the treasury departments of Britain and the United States have secretly agreed on the future value of the pound and the US dollar. Britain advocates suppressing the current value to US$4.70 per pound, while the United States insists that the price should not be lower than US$4.95. It is now believed that both sides will compromise so that the pound price fluctuates between US$4.80 and US$4.90. It is expected that the Soviet Union is deeply afraid that the value of the US dollar converted into pounds will decrease, so it sold the pound at a price of around US$5.00. (Reuters, 27th)

French National Assembly Discusses New Monetary System, Finance Committee Has Passed, Right-Wing Proposal to Postpone Rejected 33

(Paris) The National Assembly began discussing the new monetary bill this morning, and will submit it to the Senate in the evening. Therefore, the Senate is scheduled to meet at 7:00 PM to discuss it. (Havas, 28th)

(Paris) The temporary meeting of the National Assembly opened at 11:20 AM this morning to discuss the new monetary bill proposed by the government. President of the Assembly Herriot said that today's meeting is of great importance, so the audience seats are full. However, the morning meeting was only a formality, and the important discussion will have to wait until the afternoon. This morning, the first speaker was the Finance Committee reporter (Radical Socialist Party member) Schmidt, who strongly advocated the currency devaluation policy, saying that he himself had long advocated currency devaluation. After the implementation of this policy, the Bank of France would re-evaluate the value of its gold, and would obtain a profit of 16 billion francs. Of this, 10 billion francs should be used for the exchange equalization fund, and the remaining 6 billion francs should be deposited by the government in the Bank of France to repay the government's debts to the bank and increase the bank's activity capacity. This is obviously beneficial, etc. The leader of the right-wing Republican Democratic Union, former Minister without Portfolio Marran, then rose to speak and criticised the bill proposed by the government, saying that the result would put public debt holders and people receiving pensions in a difficult situation, and requested that the discussion of this bill be postponed and returned to the Finance Committee for re-examination. The Chairman put Marran's suggestion to a vote, and as a result, it was rejected by 365 votes to 248. It was 1:00 PM, and the meeting was adjourned until 4:00 PM. (Havas, 28th)

(Paris) The Finance Committee of the National Assembly met this afternoon. Finance Minister Olivar attended and explained the negotiation process of the British, French, and American monetary agreement and the content of the new monetary bill. The Finance Committee immediately voted to pass the monetary bill proposed by the government without making any modifications to the original proposal. When the Finance Committee voted on the bill, there were 20 votes in favour, 12 votes against, and 7 abstentions. The Socialist Party and the Radical Socialist Party both voted in favour, the Communist Party abstained from voting, and the central and right-wing parties all voted against. As for the temporary meetings of the Senate and the National Assembly, they are scheduled to open at 9:00 AM tomorrow, when the Radical Socialist Party member of the National Assembly Schmidt will present a report to the National Assembly on behalf of the Finance Committee. There are 15 members who plan to give speeches, including former Finance Minister Reynaud. Reynaud has great authority on financial issues, and his speech will be noticed by all parties. In addition, Finance Minister Olivar, Minister of National Economy Spinasse, and Prime Minister Léon Blum will also participate in the debate. It is expected that the debate will continue throughout the day tomorrow, and a vote cannot be held until late at night. Observers unanimously agree that the National Assembly will pass the monetary bill by a large majority, as was the case when the National Assembly passed various government bills in the past. So far, members of both houses have not proposed any amendments, because the full text of the government proposal was only revealed this afternoon, and members have not had time to study it in detail. It is expected that the easiest issues to cause disagreement will be the various economic and social bills associated with the monetary bill, and the bill on revising civil servants' salaries to make them consistent with the price index will be the focus of debate in the National Assembly. (Havas, 27th)

(Paris) The parliamentary groups of the Communist Party, the Radical Socialist Party, and the Independent Socialist Party held meetings this morning to discuss the position that their respective parliamentary groups should take on the new monetary bill. As a result, they all supported the government's proposal. Among them, the Radical Socialist Party voted in favour by 55 votes to 13. The Communist Party advocated that all amendments aimed at assisting the working class and the middle class, so as not to suffer losses due to currency devaluation, should be supported. From this point of view, the government will definitely get a majority of votes in favour of the new monetary bill in the National Assembly. (Havas, 28th)

New Monetary Law Divided Into Seven Items 34

(Paris) The main points of the new monetary bill submitted by the government to the National Assembly can be divided into the following seven points:

(1) The monetary law of June 25, 1928, stipulates that each franc contains 0.0655 grams of gold with 90% purity, and that the Bank of France has the obligation to accept paper money in exchange for cash. Both of these provisions are repealed.

(2) The gold content of the franc in the future shall be stipulated by order separately, but the weight of gold contained in each new franc shall not be less than 0.043 grams and shall not be more than 0.049 grams. In other words, the original value of the franc will be devalued by at least one-quarter and at most one-third.

(3) The purpose of the Exchange Equalisation Fund is to adjust the exchange rate of the franc against foreign currencies, so as not to exceed the restrictions stipulated in the above item.

(4) The Exchange Equalisation Fund is managed by the Bank of France on behalf of the Treasury, which is no different from the current practices in Britain and the United States.

In short, the franc will temporarily suspend cash redemption before the exchange rate is truly stable. As for the measure to stabilize the exchange rate, it may not be certain until several months or a year later. It is expected to stabilize at the same time as the pound and the US dollar.

(5) Recalculate the value of the Bank of France's gold reserves at 0.049 grams of gold with 90% purity per franc, and most of the surplus, that is, 13 billion francs, will be allocated for the Exchange Equalisation Fund.

(6) After the suspension of cash redemption of paper money, the gold market must be controlled, and the responsibility for control is given to the Bank of France.

(7) Those who possess gold bars, gold coins, and gold coins at home and abroad must report the amount of pure gold they possess to the government before October 10th, and the government will extract funds, the amount of which must be equal to the amount by which the price of gold has increased due to the devaluation of the franc.

In addition, the new monetary bill also advocates revising salaries and wages to be compatible with the price index. As for the holders of various public debts and treasury bills, they can exchange their bonds for life bonds and give a subsidy of 10% (that is, a bond with a face value of 100 francs can be exchanged for a life bond of 110 francs). Those who purchased short-term treasury bills between July 10th and September 23rd of this year shall be given considerable benefits for reconciliation. (Havas, 27th)

(Paris) This bill does not determine the legal gold content of the new franc, but only states that the gold content of the franc shall be stipulated by order in the future, which is not what our telegram expected yesterday. At the same time, the monetary bill stipulates that the minimum gold content of each franc is 0.043 grams of gold with 90% purity, and the maximum is 0.049 grams of gold with 90% purity. The original gold content of the franc was 0.0655 grams of gold with 90% purity, so this decision to devalue the franc, the percentage of its devaluation, is at least 25.19% and at most 34.36%. In other words, after the government's monetary bill is passed by the National Assembly, the franc will fall in price by at least one-quarter. The Bank of France currently has reserves of 520 billion francs. After the monetary devaluation, recalculating the franc can yield a profit of 13 billion francs. Afterwards, the franc can continue to be devalued to the maximum limit of 34.36% under the strict control of the monetary authorities. When the franc continues to be devalued, the currencies of the United States and Belgium shall also be devalued accordingly according to the monetary agreement. The government can use this method to determine the nominal value of French currency, so that it advances and retreats in the same way as the nominal value of American currency. In addition, it can be adjusted by the exchange rate balance fund. If this is the case, it will not be difficult for various currencies to achieve the ultimate goal of mutual stability. (Havas, 27th)

Spanish Government in Increasing Danger, Important Southern Town Falls Again, Government Troops Also Lose in Air War, Government Makes Final Appeal to People 36

Burgos. Spanish rebel leader General Franco issued a public statement here today, saying that the revolutionary army has now occupied the fortress of Toledo, 50 miles southwest of Madrid, and the remaining garrison in the Alcázar Fortress has been rescued. General Varela's column was the most successful in the rebel occupation of Toledo, as the team broke through the government army's front line in Maguarda, occupied the city of Torrijos, and then crossed the Guadarrama River under heavy fire. The advance guard of the team, led by Colonel Gastilon, first arrived near the Alcázar Fortress at dawn, and then charged forward in order to rescue the brave and unyielding garrison in the fortress. Before the rebels crossed the Guadarrama River, the planes of the two armies had a fierce air battle, because several government planes were ordered to fly from Madrid to Toledo to stop the rebels from advancing. Unexpectedly, they met five rebel bombers and nine fighter planes on the way. The government planes saw that they were outnumbered and tried to escape, but two of them were shot down by the rebel planes. (Reuters, 28th)

Toledo Front. General Franco's troops fought fiercely with the government army all day today and have already entered the city of Toledo. As of the time of the telegram, the war had not stopped. The rebel army is mainly composed of Moorish soldiers and Spanish foreign soldiers. They have now occupied the barracks, hospitals, bullfighting arenas, and the entire northern suburbs. The government army is still holding on to the ancient city within the city wall, including the Alcázar Fortress. The rebel army entered through the Visagra Gate and has now made contact with the troops advancing from the Guadarrama River and the Bagus West Road. (National Telegram, 27th)

Toledo. A special report from our correspondent says that the outposts of the Nationalist Army opened into the city at 1:00 PM yesterday, and a fierce street battle took place with the garrison. Half an hour later, they occupied the central area of the city. The garrison of the Alcázar Palace, seeing the rescue troops entering the city, also broke out of the siege and made contact with them. At that time, the government army was already exhausted due to heavy losses and immediately retreated to the town of West Guadalajara, retreating both on foot and by truck. Except for the area near the Alcázar Palace and the Cathedral, the rest of the city is intact, and even the Cathedral was not affected. At this moment, the avenue from the city to Madrid has been controlled by the Nationalist Army's artillery fire for several kilometers. Another column, led by General Varela, has occupied the town of Lillhof near the city of Torrijos, killing about 100 government soldiers. (Havas, 28th)

Lisbon. Spanish rebel General Trano broadcast a message on the Seville radio station yesterday, saying that Toledo had been captured today and Madrid could be captured tomorrow. However, the Madrid government authorities do not admit that the capital has been shaken. As for the rebel army's offensive plan, it does not go beyond the following two routes: one is to advance 20 miles east from Toledo, occupy Aranjuez, and cut off the railway to cut off Madrid's food supply; the other is to divide the troops into three routes and go straight to Madrid. (National Telegram, 27th)

Madrid. The Spanish government issued a letter to the people of the whole country today, the main idea being: "The government does not want to hide anything about the facts. It is our duty to inform the people that the enemy has promised our national land to foreign countries in advance, in order to obtain a large supply of foreign weapons. Now, relying on the superiority of these weapons, they are making their best efforts to advance on Madrid, the capital of the Republic. Madrid is now the core of the anti-fascist struggle. The establishment of the Republican system and the heroic battle against the enemy have all come from the leadership of Madrid. For this reason, the fascist flames and the inhuman rebels will not be happy until they destroy Madrid... Now, only by saving the crisis in Madrid with all our strength can we liberate the entire Spanish nation from the oppression of the Fascist Party. All Republican and anti-fascist families, regardless of Catalan, Basque, Galician, Valencian, and Andalusian, all Spaniards with honor and blood should immediately rise up to participate in the defense of Madrid, and should make preparations in advance, so that even in the event of an accident, they can have something to rely on and be fearless. Although the future is full of difficulties, our heroic people are still blocking the rebel army's path, preventing them from attacking the capital. However, in order to make our efforts more effective, various anti-enemy troops must adjust their actions, abide by military discipline, and obey their leaders before they can be effective," and so on. Rural Life Talks: The Economic Life of the Yao People of Dateng Mountain in Guangxi: Forms of Mountain Rent and Extra Contributions 52

— Edited by Yu Qingtang, Written by Tang Zhaomin

Whenever I enter the villages of the Yao people, some mountain laborers inevitably complain to me. When it comes to the ferocious mountain landlords, they always shake their heads and sigh. Originally, in Yao Mountain society, mountain landlords are like feudal lords, and mountain laborers are like serfs. Feudal lords have land, so political privileges are completely in their hands; mountain laborers entrust their lives to the land of the mountain landlords, so how can they not be controlled and exploited by them? Just looking at the forms of mountain rent, there are some shocking things: Some pay rent in products, with the income from the mountains accounting for one-third of the output; some pay rent in poultry, with each house site or tomb site, or a section of fishing or hunting ground, required to pay two catties of live chickens each year; some pay rent in currency, generally requiring the equivalent of one-fifth to one-third of the output. In addition, there is also the "labor compensation system" of using labor to pay mountain rent; or when the mountain landlord is too far away from the mountain land and it is difficult for the mountain laborers to send the products to the door, there is also "rent conversion" of converting the rent into currency; there is also a method of calculating rent based on population, that is, the mountain laborers who cultivate the mountain fields, regardless of the size of the land they cultivate (in fact, there are natural restrictions), and the abundance or scarcity of the harvest, all men aged between fifteen and sixty must pay eight jiao of rent silver per person; in some places, the rent is calculated by household, with each household required to pay one yuan—this kind of mountain rent form similar to "poll tax" or "household tax" is only practiced in Huangqian, Liumiao, Hongtai, Luoxi, which belong to Xiang County, and Dongwen, which belongs to Wuyi County. These things are really too bizarre. The mountain laborers are bound by the mountain landlords' chains of layered exploitation, and there is no way to struggle to break free. They only cry as they speak, and we can only sigh as we listen.

As for the general forms of mountain rent: Among the rent in kind, there are two types: share rent and fixed rent. Generally speaking, share rent is more prevalent than fixed rent; the reason is that mountain field reclamation cannot be fertilized as a rule, and due to the relationship of land fertility, the yield in the first year and the second year differs greatly. Therefore, it is not easy to determine the fixed rent. Methods of renting land: Some are agreed upon verbally, and some have written contracts; some do not specify the term of the lease, and some specify a certain period. There is also a "forever long lease" of perpetual tenancy. Generally, the most common is not specifying a term, and the least common is the forever long lease. Those that do not specify a term are often agreed upon verbally; those with a term and perpetual tenancy are mostly written contracts. However, nine out of ten of these contracts are written by Han Chinese on their behalf. Han Chinese can get a "benefit" for writing contracts for them! A writing fee.

In some places, there are also names such as "first installment rent" and "flowing rent." The so-called first installment is to pay a large sum of money to the mountain landlord before renting the mountain land, and then stipulate the amount of rent and set a time limit. Some only pay the first installment once, and no longer pay it afterward; some, in addition to paying the first installment, have to pay a small amount of rent each year—this rent that is paid separately each year is called "flowing rent," or, in contrast to the first installment, it is specifically called the "final installment." The former has the meaning of a pledge, while the latter has a stronger tenancy nature. Although this form of mountain rent with the payment of a first installment can slightly improve the status of the mountain laborers, the mountain laborers pay a large sum of money before they can make a profit, which is very uneconomical.

I have repeatedly asked mountain laborers, which of the various mountain rents is the most suitable? The answer obtained to this question can be summarized in one sentence: it is convenient for the mountain landlords, and the mountain laborers suffer losses. In other words, no matter what form of mountain rent it is, it makes it difficult for the mountain laborers to bear. In fact, the exploitation of the mountain landlords is not only limited to these various mountain rents. In reality, in addition to paying the above-mentioned various mountain rents as usual, the mountain laborers also have various extra supplies to the mountain landlords. Below, let's record the words of Zhao Ruxiang, the head of the Yao people in Guicun, Hongtai Ridge, complaining to me:

"The Yao people, who have become mountain laborers of the Changmao Yao, will never have a bright future in their lives! They are exhausted to death, and they are poor to death! They plant fields, and we plant mountains; every time it comes to the time of demarcation, they want us to help them with their work. We are planting their mountains, who dares not to go? We have to leave our own work undone and help them with their work. By the time we have finished their work, our own farming has passed its season... This is fine, but what is most hateful is that when the mountain landlord comes to our house, he starts calling "boy" and ends calling "boy". We have to treat him with good wine and good food, letting him eat and drink as much as he wants. Eating is not enough, if he sees something that pleases him, he asks for it as soon as he opens his mouth, and takes it as soon as he reaches out his hand. Whether it's chickens, ducks, small dishes, or miscellaneous grains, he has to take some back with him before he can be satisfied. Also, when approving the mountain, they want us to prepare "mountain opening wine"; when sending rent, we also have to bring some wine, rice, and pork to show respect to him. What's even more outrageous is that in some places where cedar and paulownia can be planted, the mountain landlord wants us to "plant trees to return the mountain" (Note 1)!"

My temperament is somewhat impatient, and when I heard him say that it was too pitiful, I interjected, "It's enough for the mountain landlord to want rent, why do they do this kind of nonsense? This is really unreasonable, you can refuse him!" Who knew that before I finished speaking, he shook his head and said, "Sir, you don't know how evil they are! If you don't give it to him, he will scold you if he doesn't beat you. Sometimes, being beaten and scolded is not a big deal, you still have to be fined! Mountain laborers who are not respectful to mountain landlords are violating the "stone tablet" (Note 2). If you don't comply, he will immediately take back the mountain field and tell you to get out."

...We were all silent for a while, and he continued, "Sir, are you angry when you hear these things? You don't know that in some places—for example, in the Liudu Liuding area of Xiuren—mountain laborers even have to pay ten catties, eight catties, or even hundreds of catties of pork to the mountain landlord when they marry a wife!"

When Xiang said this, he almost burst into tears. In fact, not only did he tell me this, but all mountain laborers said the same thing in unison. I thought of the relations of production under the feudal system, and I thought of the extra-economic oppression that landlords often exerted on serfs, so I had to shut up and remain silent.

Note 1: The mountain landlord approves a piece of land to a mountain laborer. The first year is for clearing and planting. In the spring of the second year, the mountain landlord wants the mountain laborer to insert cedar branches on the ground for him to propagate. Some are also planted by the mountain landlord himself, or he sows paulownia seeds himself. But whether the mountain landlord plants them himself or the mountain laborer helps him plant them, the responsibility for protecting them is entirely borne by the mountain laborer. If one of them dies, the mountain laborer must replant it. If a slightly larger tree is hoeed to death, he will also be fined a few cents. After four or five years, the trees will become a forest. This land can no longer be planted and must be returned to the mountain landlord. The mountain laborer cannot share any of the benefits of the trees.

Note 2: There is a primitive political organization in Yao Mountain called the Stone Tablet, that is, a village or several villages, or even dozens of villages, unite and erect a stone in an open space. They sacrifice a pig as a sacrifice to it. After the sacrifice, each drinks a cup of blood wine to show solidarity. The head of the Stone Tablet (i.e., the leader) will announce the rules in public, and everyone must abide by them afterward. The mountain laborer class sometimes participates in various matters, but has no right to speak. They only carefully abide by what the mountain landlords have agreed upon.

Ministries of Communications and Railways Plan to Build New Jinghan Express Ship 63

Connecting Tianjin-Pukou, Shanghai-Nanjing, Pinghan, and Yuehan Four Routes 64

Implementing Joint Water-Land Transportation for Traveler Convenience 65

Hankou Communication: The Ministries of Communications and Railways have made considerable achievements in developing transportation in recent years. The completion of the Yuehan Railway this time has broken the isolated situation of the two Guangdong provinces at once, and its contribution is especially noteworthy. In order to complete the joint water-land transportation, it is striving to connect the Pinghan, Yuehan, Tianjin-Pukou, and Shanghai-Nanjing lines. The Pinghan, Yuehan, Tianjin-Pukou, and Shanghai-Nanjing lines also take Hankou and Nanjing as hubs. The Jinghan route is connected by the Yangtze River. In terms of ship transportation, there should be special equipment and speed to cope with the environment. At present, the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Yangtze River ships, such as the Jiang'an, Jiangshun, Jianghua, and Jiangxin, although their equipment and speed are better than other ships, are still difficult to shoulder this important task. The Ministries of Communications and Railways have proposed to build a new Jinghan express ship. The plan has been drafted and is expected to be implemented. A brief outline is recorded below, which is also a noteworthy page in the history of transportation.

Shipbuilding Design: The length of the ships currently sailing on the Yangtze River is 340 feet at most. The length of the express ship is set at 300 feet, so that when the Yangtze River is low, there will be no difficulties in sailing. The total capacity is roughly limited to 3,000 tons. The cargo is from 300 tons to 400 tons. In addition to the rooms used by the crew, the passenger cabins should be able to accommodate at least the following number of passengers: 20 in the special class, 40 in the first class, 200 in the second class, and 600 in the ordinary class. As for the speed, the minimum speed upstream is 12 nautical miles, and the downstream speed is 16.5 nautical miles. The draft depth should not exceed 11 feet when fully loaded, so that it can sail in winter.

Shipping Line and Schedule: The Jinghan express ship will run exclusively between Nanjing and Hankou, passing through Jiujiang, Anqing, etc., each stopping for half an hour to allow passengers to board and disembark. The schedule stipulates that it will depart from Nanjing on Mondays and Thursdays, and from Hankou on Wednesdays and Saturdays. The ship will stay in Beijing for one day of the week. It is found that Nanjing to Anqing is 158 nautical miles, Anqing to Jiujiang is 90 nautical miles, and Jiujiang to Hankou is 139 nautical miles. If the express ship's upstream speed is 12 nautical miles, then Nanjing to Anqing will take 13 hours and 10 minutes, Anqing to Jiujiang will take 7.5 hours, and Jiujiang to Hankou will take 11.5 hours. It is estimated that it will take 32 hours and 10 minutes to travel from Nanjing to Hankou. Assuming that the berthing time in Anqing and Jiujiang is 1 hour and 45 minutes, then it will take 34 hours for the express ship to go upstream from Nanjing to Hankou. If the downstream speed is set at 16.5 nautical miles, then it will take 8.5 hours from Hankou to Jiujiang. The travel time from Hankou to Nanjing is 24 hours. Assuming that the berthing in Jiujiang and Anqing is 1 hour, it will take 25 hours to go downstream from Hankou to Nanjing.

Budget Estimate: Regarding the expenditure, one is the start-up fee, the shipbuilding material cost is estimated at 900,000 yuan, and the ship's passenger equipment is estimated at 100,000 yuan, for a total of 1 million yuan. The other is the operating cost: (1) The salary and food of the driving engine workers is estimated at 3,700 yuan per month, totaling 44,400 yuan per year. (2) The food of the employees of the administrative department is 2,500 yuan, totaling 30,000 yuan per year. (3) The repair cost is 16,000 yuan per year. (4) The interest on the ship's capital is about 50,000 yuan per year, calculated at 5%. (5) The depreciation of the ship's capital is 5%, which is 50,000 yuan. (6) The insurance is 3%, which is 30,000 yuan. (7) Gold sundries are 1,200 yuan per month, totaling 14,400 yuan per year. (8) Coal, the weekly budget is 320 tons, estimated at 4,000 yuan. Excluding the repair period, it is calculated at 48 weeks per year, which requires 192,000 yuan. (9) Tonnage tax, loading and unloading fees for passengers and cargo, and miscellaneous items, totaling 10,000 yuan per year. The total annual operating expenses are estimated at 436,800 yuan. Regarding income, A. 20 special class passengers, 36 yuan per person, totaling 720 yuan. B. 40 first-class passengers, 16 yuan per person, totaling 640 yuan. C. 200 second-class passengers, 10 yuan per person, totaling 2,000 yuan. D. 600 ordinary-class passengers, 4 yuan per person, totaling 2,400 yuan. The above totals 5,760 yuan. Calculated at 50%, the passenger revenue per trip is 2,380 yuan. Also, due to short-distance passengers, etc., the net amount is calculated at 85% of the above number, which is 2,023 yuan. There are four round trips per week, totaling 8,092 yuan. Calculated at 48 weeks per year, the total is 388,416 yuan. In addition, the freight for goods and mail is estimated at 500 yuan per week, totaling 24,000 yuan per year. Therefore, the total annual revenue from passenger tickets and freight is 410,416 yuan. The above expenditure totals 436,800 yuan, and the revenue totals 410,416 yuan. It is estimated that there will be a loss of 26,384 yuan per year.

Cooperation Method: The cost of shipbuilding is estimated at 1 million yuan per ship. The Ministry of Railways and the Ministry of Communications will each build one ship first, that is, use the remaining amount of the materials ordered for the new ship built by the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company in the Gengzi Indemnity Loan the year before last. The wage portion will be raised by the Ministry separately. However, according to the distribution of shipping money, three ships are required to have one ship departing from Beijing and Hankou every day. However, two ships will be piloted first. The third ship is planned to be built after the negotiation with a German merchant to borrow materials. The joint transportation method of this express ship will be determined by the Ministry of Communications in consultation with the Ministry of Railways with reference to the successful cases of water-land joint transportation in various places. The main purpose of setting up the express ship is to connect with the Pinghan, Yuehan, Tianjin-Pukou, and Shanghai-Nanjing railways. The schedules of all railways and express ships should be discussed with the relevant railway bureaus for a long-term plan to achieve perfection and benefit travelers. However, the expenses of the express ship are very large, especially the item of coal. Since the Ministry of Communications is cooperating with the Ministry of Railways, the freight for coal, regardless of where it is purchased, will be calculated at half the rate for all railway transportation in accordance with regulations, in order to maintain career transportation. (September 27)

Cancellation of the Fujian Tax Inspection Office Great Success of Smuggling Suppression in Four Months Fujian and Xiamen Have Been Severely Attacked by a Certain Party 66

Xiamen Communication: The Fujian Provincial Government established the Provincial Tax Inspection Office in May and set up 18 inspection branch offices in important coastal ports to cooperate with the customs patrol ships in suppressing smuggling by land and water. After four months, the effect has just begun to show. On September 19, the provincial government suddenly ordered all of them to be revoked. Fujian Province and Taiwan are separated by a strip of water. From Changle and Lianjiang in the north to Xiamen and Zhangpu in the south, they face each other across the sea. The narrowest point is only 70 nautical miles, and can be navigated by a small boat. Therefore, smuggled goods are loaded from Taiwan by sailboats or paddle boats and driven directly to the coastal ports for unloading. The second half of last year was the most prosperous. Almost all the white sugar was smuggled. In January, the Xiamen Customs officially reported that only a few hundred catties were imported for tax purposes. In addition, kerosene, cloth, seafood, matches, and groceries were also major items. From July last year to April this year, it is estimated that the total value of smuggled goods imported into the jurisdiction of Xiamen Customs in ten months was no less than 5 million yuan. Last winter, Xiamen Customs submitted a report to the General Taxation Department to increase the number of patrol ships to patrol the coast in sections. Many cases were detected. The confiscated goods were auctioned in Shanghai, and the ships were dismantled, which suffered considerable blows. However, the customs can only reach the sea. Most of the smuggling is done by coastal merchants colluding with local bullies. If they can break through the patrol ship's logical seizure of money, they can travel unimpeded. Moreover, smugglers also privately set up radio stations to communicate with each other and peep at the actions of patrol ships, waiting for the opportunity to cross quickly, so they have not been slightly suppressed. The establishment of the provincial government's inspection office is specifically responsible for land smuggling suppression, which complements the customs. The joint investigation by land and water has been effective for four months. In August, Xiamen Customs' import tax reached more than 930,000 yuan, breaking this year's record, which can be a clear proof. However, this also aroused repercussions, starting in Fuzhou and then in Xiamen. Last month, the inspection office conducted an inspection of smuggled goods in shops in Fuzhou City, which greatly opposed a certain party. In order to cope with the environment, the provincial government recently ordered the inspection office to revoke the Changle, Hui'an, and Shima branch offices. Xia Sheng, the director of the inspection office, immediately submitted a report to the provincial government on the 19th, requesting the complete revocation of the inspection office and its branch offices, which was approved by the provincial government and notified all branch offices in the province to end on September 25. The order stated, "According to the report submitted by Xia Sheng, the director of the Provincial Tax Inspection Office, the office has financial difficulties, and smuggling has gradually subsided recently. There is no need to establish the office. Please revoke it to emphasize public funds." It has been found that this is true and should be approved for revocation. In addition to ordering the office and all tax bureaus to know and handle it, it is ordered to transfer the order to all branch offices for compliance. The Xiamen Office was established for only 19 days, and the work was stopped upon receiving the order, and it ended at the same time on the 25th. The office cracked a case on the 15th night where sailors of the Yixian warship smuggled sugar. The Quanzhou 12th branch office, together with the Quanzhou sub-customs, cracked a smuggling agency in Xunpu outside the city on the 13th, which are the most notable events in southern Fujian recently.

Anhui North Tobacco Leaf Bumper Harvest Now on the Market Concentrated in Mentai 67

Bengbu Communication: The Fengyang and Dingyuan in northern Anhui. The Huaiyuan area has fertile soil and abundant products. In addition to the five grains, tobacco leaves are the most important. The production in Fengjing is the largest. It is the only by-product of farmers. Every autumn, when tobacco leaves come on the market, the famous major tobacco companies send personnel to set up warehouses to purchase and transport them. Used as raw materials for cigarette making, and the British Yizhong Tobacco Company (formerly known as the British-American Tobacco Company) also has a large-scale smoking factory in Mentai Zi, which purchases them every autumn. The income of tobacco farmers is several million yuan, which is used to adjust the rural economy. The Tobacco Tax Management Office receives the most smoking tax every year, up to more than 600,000 yuan. This year, the weather is good, and the tobacco leaves have a bumper harvest. They have now come on the market one after another. Here is a brief record of the production and sales of tobacco areas.

Production Area: The original soil tobacco in Fengyang was promoted by the compradors of the British-American Tobacco Company during the 89th year of the Republic of China, and American tobacco leaves were planted and improved. Tobacco farmers made huge profits. By the 12th and 13th years of the Republic of China, more and more people planted them, and the price also increased. The average value of each hundred pounds was 20 yuan. At that time, the tobacco companies that purchased tobacco leaves included British-American, Nanyang, Flag, and Huacheng tobacco companies. Later, the value gradually decreased, and Nanyang. Huacheng stopped buying one after another. Now the market is almost completely monopolized by Yizhong. Because of the strong foreign capital, no Chinese tobacco company can compete with it. Fengyang is the most common production area, followed by Dingyuan. Huaiyuan is second. In addition, there are also planters in counties such as Shou County. Su County. Lingbi. Wuhe, etc., but the number is small. According to statistics, there are more than 40,000 tobacco farmers in several counties.

Sowing: Most of the tobacco leaves in the counties are American varieties, and the soil varieties have been gradually eliminated. The sowing time is in March in spring. The seeds are scattered in specially opened garden ridges. Before the Minor Fullness, the tobacco seedlings have grown four or five inches long. At this time, they are transplanted into the fields, just like transplanting rice seedlings. Tobacco fields must be given considerable fertilizer to facilitate growth. The work of cultivating, weeding, and removing insects is also very繁劇。 Tobacco leaves are warm and should be mild. They are afraid of drought and especially afraid of waterlogging.

Harvest: By mid-July, the leaves gradually grow up. The tobacco farmers gradually pick them from the bottom to the top of the stems and place them in the pit room to bake them. The large pit room can bake 500 catties each time, and the small one can bake 300 catties each time. Each time, it takes four or five days to dry. At this time, they are transported out of the pit room and placed on the ground to be slightly exposed to dew to make them soft. Then they are collected indoors and selected manually, divided into grades, and transported to the market for sale.

Yield: The maximum yield of tobacco leaves per mu can reach more than 35 market catties. The larger the yield, the better the quality. Otherwise, the quality of tobacco is inferior. The income from selling tobacco per mu is more than 100 yuan, and less than only a few yuan. As for the cost, each mu requires 45 yuan of fertilizer, and the coal for baking accounts for 2 yuan. In total, the average cost of planting and harvesting per mu is more than 10 yuan. Therefore, tobacco farmers sometimes lose money. After the tobacco leaves come on the market, they are tied into bundles by tobacco farmers and transported to the market. Bengbu has a tobacco leaf market. Tobacco companies such as Fuchang and Dalai mostly purchase in Bengbu. The market opens in September every year. This question is because no one has purchased it recently, so it has not been weighed yet. However, Mentai Zi has Yizhong Tobacco Company setting up a factory to purchase, and it has now been weighed. A large number of tobacco leaves from all directions are transported and concentrated in Mentai every day. Shouldering burdens, carrying donkeys, and boxes are endless, and the market is suddenly lively. Social finance is also suddenly active. The recent tobacco market seems to be between 6 yuan and 40 yuan per dan. Because the quality of tobacco is good or bad, the price is very different. The Bengbu Tobacco Tax Management Office's Mentai smoking tax collection office collects taxes at the factory, and the daily income is considerable.

Wu Manufacturing: When Yizhong Tobacco Company in Mentai Zi purchases tobacco leaves, it purchases them on one side and re-smokes them on the other side. There are smoking machines in the factory, and a large number of workers are hired to smoke them in the factory every day. They are divided into grades and packed in specially made large wooden barrels, which can prevent corrosion and remain unchanged for a long time. Stacks are stacked like mountains in the warehouse. As soon as next year's spring comes, they will be loaded into cars and transported to Shanghai to make cigarettes and distributed to various places at home and abroad.

Songjiang Please Exempt Housing Donations 68

The county investigated the housing donations, and the county chamber of commerce previously telegraphed the provincial government, cherishing the people's livelihood, and requested that it be exempted. British Correspondence Establishment of the Anglo-Egyptian Military Alliance Treaty 80

— Feng Lieshan

Judging from the contents of this treaty, the Egyptian independence movement, which has been fought for over the years, has largely been successful. The only thing the British have not relaxed their grip on is the military power in the Suez Canal area. The rest, to a greater or lesser extent, can be considered a major concession. Egypt is establishing this treaty with Britain as an independent country. From now on, it will be a country completely equal to Britain. According to the treaty, both sides will send ambassadors to each other. Britain will help Egypt apply to join the League of Nations and obtain membership. At the same time, Britain has also agreed to abolish extraterritorial rights in Egypt and withdraw troops to within the Suez Canal area. In short, the British feel that this time they are truly a nation that could not be any greater!

The most important points of the treaty are as follows:

Suez Canal Garrison Issue British troops will soon begin to move from the Egyptian interior to the Suez Canal area. Egypt recognizes Britain's right to protect the Suez Canal. The number of British troops is stipulated at 10,000, plus airmen and crew, for a term of 20 years. If circumstances change after 20 years and Egypt wants to reclaim its power, this dispute will be decided by the League of Nations.

However, the British withdrawal of troops from the Egyptian interior is not unconditional. The Egyptian government must build four 20-foot-wide military roads between the Egyptian interior and the Suez Canal area, and three railway lines must be renovated or have their gauge changed. In addition, barracks must be built for the British garrison in the Suez Canal area. Only after Egypt fully fulfills these conditions will Britain begin to withdraw its troops. Because after all these transportation issues are resolved, these 10,000 British troops will still have great military significance in Egypt. In addition, British aircraft can freely fly over Egyptian territory in peacetime, and British troops can be stationed everywhere in wartime, with the Egyptian government having no right to interfere. It can be seen that the British are unwilling to concede much in military matters.

Several Egyptian Victories The Egyptian army, which has historically been under British control, will be completely reorganized. British officers serving in the army will all resign and be replaced by Egyptians. However, Britain will send a military advisory group to help the Egyptian government train the new army. From now on, Egypt will officially have its own national defense forces. However, military equipment is limited to being purchased within the British Empire. Secondly, not only judicial power, but also administrative power, will be fully recovered. The Europeans in the Egyptian government's Ministry of Interior, which were originally a disguised form of extraterritoriality, will be abolished, and the British serving in the Egyptian police will also be given a time limit to retire. The consultant system in public institutions will be abolished. As for the existing consultants, whether they leave or stay after the expiration of their contracts will be at the discretion of the Egyptian government. All this proves that Egypt has in fact gained independence, and not just in name. Because the Egyptians already have full power to manage their own affairs.

In addition, there is one point that shows that the British are indeed showing sincerity in resolving the Egyptian issue this time, hoping to win over the hearts of the Egyptians in preparation for future disasters. Negotiations between Britain and Egypt have been fruitless for years, mostly because the Anglo-Egyptian Sudan issue has been an obstacle. This time, the British have made almost complete concessions on the Sudan issue. The relationship between Sudan and Egypt will return to the situation in 1924. Egyptian troops will soon enter Sudanese territory. The status of Egyptians in Sudan will also be equal to that of the British. This can probably satisfy the Egyptians, at least in the eyes of the British. The British have built a defense line on the Suez Canal, and there is no domestic worry for at least a decade or two. On the other hand, especially in the past year, various countries have joined the arms race. Britain is not only a heavy industry country, but also has special advantages over others. Although Britain is constantly declaring in parliament and newspapers that its military strength is insufficient, this argument has gradually aroused suspicion. Recently, German newspapers have even pointed out that Britain's gradual increase in military strength is one of the reasons for the current European unrest. It can be seen that Britain has reached a considerable level of preparation.

The British Empire may collapse in a future war, but whoever strikes her first will not necessarily gain any advantage. (September 5th)
