Local News

The Bankers Association Held a Special Members' Meeting Yesterday to Discuss Procedures for Levying Income Tax Resolved to First Collect Opinions from Various Banks and Then Hold Another Meeting 81

The Ministry of Finance is conducting income tax on securities and deposit interest income. The banking sector has requested a postponement, but has received an order from the ministry that it is not approved. The Direct Tax Office has also telegraphed the Bankers Association to immediately send out various forms. However, the association believes that there are many difficulties in handling the procedures. Therefore, it held a special members' meeting yesterday to discuss the matter. As a result, it was decided to collect opinions and continue the research. The details are as follows:

Ministry of Finance Approval

The Bankers Association of this city believes that income tax is about to be implemented and there are difficulties in the procedures. After detailed research by the Bankers Association, it has formulated about 20 suggestions and once discussed them with Liang Jingchun of the Central Direct Tax Office. At the same time, the president of the association requested the Ministry of Finance to allow a postponement before a concrete plan is decided. Yesterday, the association received an approval from the Ministry of Finance, stating that the income tax levy has been promulgated and implemented by the National Government and should not be postponed. The request should not be discussed. After receiving the order, the association immediately informed all member banks.

Direct Tax Office Telegram

The Central Direct Tax Office also telegraphed the Bankers Association, saying that Lin Kanghou and the executive committee members are aware that the deposit interest income tax is about to be levied. All withholding taxes, applicable forms, and collection guidelines have been printed and will be sent to your association for distribution within days. Please notify all colleagues to prepare everything in advance. This matter is related to the reform of the tax system internally and international observation externally. I hope that you will cooperate and support it. The Preparatory Office of the Central Direct Tax Office of the Ministry of Finance respectfully. The association also immediately forwarded it to various banks to follow.

Collecting Opinions

The association held a special members' meeting at 3:00 PM yesterday. The members' representatives present were Li Fusun, Hu Xi'an, Zhang Peishen, Wang Yansong, Pan Jiufen, Wu Yunzhai, Yang Jiemei, Bei Lusun, Zhu Huisheng, Zhou Jianjie, Wang Shengeng, Luo Bokan, Jin Boming, Tong Sidao, Zhu Runsheng, Zhou Wusan, Lin Yibo, Chen Qinglai, Zhou Yaoping, Ye Gongshan, Zhou Jiyun, Xia Gongxiang, Sun Jingxi, Gong Rongdi, Zhang Zhuyu, Yuan Mengqin, Ye Daxia, Pei Zhenyong, Gan Zhuping, Mao Shouwei, Wang Zihou, Ren Fengnan, Chen Zaiming, Wang Shaoxian, Zhao Chichang, Sun Ruihuang, Luo Qinghua, Wei Zhuquan, etc. Wu Yunzhai presided over the meeting. After reporting the ministry's order, he proposed to formulate opinions and submit them for discussion. It was decided to distribute them to various banks for research and collect opinions before holding another meeting to discuss them. According to the reporter's investigation, the association decided to obey the ministry's order, but in fact, it may not be able to handle it on schedule. It was decided to request the ministry's understanding.

Association's Opinions

The opinions on income tax proposed by the Bankers Association are as follows: (1) To request an explanation of the provisional regulations and detailed rules of income tax: (A) Regarding banks: (1) Interest income from public bonds and securities purchased by banks should be exempt from income tax. (2) Interbank deposits should be exempt from taxation. (3) Interest on inter-branch transfers should be exempt from taxation. (4) Whether the public reserve funds that should be deducted from operating income include all types of public reserve funds. (5) It is proposed to exempt bank books from being submitted as evidence. (6) Please exempt banks from notifying depositors when withholding income tax. (7) Bank dividends should be subject to income tax deduction. (8) For various tax-exempt deposits, it should be stated that the bank is not responsible for identification. (B) Regarding customers: (1) Current accounts of shops should be exempt from taxation to avoid duplication. (2) The method of paying income tax for fixed deposits with withdrawals and withdrawals with fixed deposits should be stipulated. (C) Regarding employees. (D) Regarding other aspects: (1) How should bonuses, annuities, and other similar income of people engaged in various industries be taxed?

Revision of Various Points

(2) To request revision of the income tax regulations and detailed rules: (A) Regarding banks. (B) Regarding customers: (1) The tax on income from deposit interest should be differentiated and reduced, and foreign banks should be taxed uniformly. (2) Please set a tax-free limit for income from deposit interest. (C) Regarding employees: (1) Income tax should be levied starting from an income of 100 or 50 yuan, and allowances should be deducted separately and calculated in real terms. (3) Interest on insurance savings, pension funds, etc. should be exempted from tax according to Article 14 of the implementing rules. (D) Regarding other aspects: (1) Article 1, Category 1, all income from companies, shops, firms, factories, or individual capital should be changed to income from profits above "5,000" yuan. (2) Article 2, Item 2, pensions, retirement funds, and alimony for people engaged in various industries should be exempt from tax. (3) Article 3 should be amended as follows: (1) For income that is "10%" to less than "15%" of the actual capital amount, the tax rate is "10" per thousand. (2) For income that is "15%" to less than "20%" of the actual capital amount, the tax rate is "20" per thousand. (3) For income that is "20%" to less than "25%" of the actual capital amount, the tax rate is 40 per thousand. (4) For income that is "25%" to less than "30%" of the actual capital amount, the tax rate is 60 per thousand. (4) For income that is "30%" or more of the actual capital amount, the tax rate is uniformly 80 per thousand. (5) Please explain separately and supplement the regulations on tax-exempt matters for people engaged in various industries. (5) Pure profits used to make up for losses should be exempt from tax. (6) Whether the cost of supporting family members should be exempted from tax in accordance with the alimony for those who cannot make a living.

Money Industry Conference

The Money Industry Association has decided to organize an income tax research association to collect opinions from various banks and study the implementation methods in detail regarding the collection of income tax. In addition to the six people already nominated, Pei Yunqing, Qian Yuansheng, Wang Huailian, Liu Wuqiao, Lu Shuchen, and Yan Dayou, there are three more people who need to be elected by the members' representative standing committee. It is learned that the association has scheduled a members' representative standing committee meeting on October 2nd to elect three representatives to participate in the research association in order to start the research as soon as possible. The notice has been sent out yesterday.

What I Saw Yesterday The Situation in the Hongkou and Zhabei Areas Japanese Soldiers Are Withdrawing and Stationing in Succession Old Buildings and Factories Are Patrolling Separately 87

According to the Central News Agency, the situation in the Hongkou and Zhabei areas was still stable yesterday. At the intersection of Haining Road and Wusong Road in the Public Concession, the place where the Japanese sailors were attacked on the 23rd of this month, five or six Japanese military vehicles loaded with armed soldiers patrolled yesterday morning around 10:00 AM. An armored vehicle was parked in front of the Japanese military detachment of the Yongfeng Building on North Sichuan Road. One or two Japanese soldiers were still stationed at each important intersection. The Japanese elementary school resumed classes as usual yesterday morning. Several Japanese soldiers were stationed in front of the school gate. There were no Japanese soldiers in the Bazibang area of Zhabei. Even the five Japanese soldiers stationed at the Japanese cemetery returned to the camp yesterday morning. The situation of the Japanese soldiers stationed in the Japanese brewery behind the 63 Flower Garden was the same as yesterday. The reporter went to watch at a distance of about a dozen steps from the factory yesterday morning, which proves that the rumors that the Japanese army was building projects next to the factory are not accurate. There were about dozens of Japanese soldiers stationed in the factory. A shed made of corrugated iron was set up next to the factory for vehicles to park. The land of the factory is mostly owned by the Japanese. This time, because the Japanese army's housing was not enough, dozens of them were temporarily moved here and will be moved out soon. A reporter from Xinsheng News Agency discovered dozens of Japanese soldiers stationed at the intersections of Diswei Road and Qimei Road, and Ouyang Road and Sida Road yesterday. According to the investigation results, the Japanese soldiers at the intersection of Diswei Road and Qimei Road are stationed in a foreign house at No. 1097, with about 60 to 70 people. They were moved here from the intersection of Tiantong Road and Diswei Road. At the former site of the Yuenae Garden in the same place, the Japanese army is building on a large scale. It is learned that the construction plan was before the Japanese soldier case on Wusong Road, but construction started from the day before yesterday. It is a military officer's dormitory. As for the Japanese soldiers at the intersection of Ouyang Road and Sida Road, they are stationed in a Japanese girls' school, with about 80 people. These two places are similar to the Yongfeng Building at Xingjiaqiao on North Sichuan Road, belonging to the nature of a detachment. There are also armored vehicles, motorcycles, and military trucks stationed there, which patrol Diswei Road and Qimei Road from time to time. Gather at the wasteland of the old Baoshan Glass Factory at the end of Huayuan Street and the Japanese brewery. The number of Japanese soldiers is indeed close to 200.

At about 9:00 AM yesterday morning, a reporter from Xinsheng News Agency also saw a small team of Japanese soldiers, about a dozen people, taking a No. 9 truck and driving straight south across the Sichuan Road Bridge, passing Nanjing Road and heading west, seemingly heading to the west of Shanghai. The Yongfeng Building has been leased by the Japanese army as a detachment. Yesterday, there were still two trucks, one armored vehicle, and one motorcycle parked in front of the building, and five or six guards were stationed on the sidewalk in front of the building.

Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society: Paper Presentations Continued Yesterday Morning; Adjournment in the Afternoon; Banquet Hosted by Minister of Finance Kong in the Evening; Meeting of Society Affairs at Mayor's Banquet Today 89

The 13th annual meeting of the Chinese Economic Society, which opened the day before yesterday, continued yesterday morning at 9:00 AM in the East Hall on the ninth floor of the YMCA, with the presentation of members' papers. The meeting adjourned in the afternoon, and in the evening, the Central Bank hosted a banquet. Paper presentations will continue this morning, and at noon, Mayor Wu will host a banquet, followed by a meeting of the society's affairs at the City Hall, and a visit to various architectural projects in the city center. A public banquet by various cultural organizations will be held in the evening. Details are as follows:

Paper Presentations

Yesterday morning at 9:00 AM, the meeting continued in the East Hall on the ninth floor of the YMCA, with the presentation of members' papers. Tang Qingzeng represented and Li Zhaohuan presided over the meeting, saying, "The scope of the members' papers this time, in view of the nation's difficulties and the people's hardship, and to adapt to the current situation, the topics of the papers all focus on the two major principles of 'Economic Problems in Extraordinary Times' and 'Fiscal Problems in Extraordinary Times,' which is extremely important. A total of fifteen papers have been received this time, all of which are carefully structured. However, the members' ideas are not completely the same, so the agenda of the conference has specially set a longer time for the presentation of papers, in order to learn from each other, get accurate conclusions, and contribute to the government to cope with extraordinary times." The chairman announced the rules for the presentation of papers: 20 minutes for presentation and 15 minutes for discussion, in order. Member Yao Tiexin first presented "On War Economics," followed by Li Quanshi's "The Problem of Implementing Income Tax in China," Zhang Sumin's "Peace Economy and Extraordinary Times Economy," and Xiong Lingxiao's "Finance in Extraordinary Times." After each member's paper presentation, they provided as many opinions as possible, learning from each other and attacking. Especially on the upcoming implementation of the income tax issue, many refined opinions were expressed. The remaining papers will continue to be presented this morning.

Main Points of the Papers

(1) Ma Yinchu on the issue of commodity prices and paper currency policies in extraordinary times: First, he described the commodity price system in extraordinary times, and that China cannot adopt the methods of Europe and the United States in the economic center of the European War and the control of commodity prices. The final conclusion is that in extraordinary times, all necessities for life and military use should adopt a quantitative distribution method. In terms of finance, it is absolutely necessary not to adopt a paper currency policy to promote the soaring of commodity prices. New taxes should be raised, such as income tax and inheritance tax that do not increase the burden on farmers, to supplement. (2) Li Quanshi on the problem of implementing income tax in China, expressed great approval of the principles of income tax, but worried that the good tax of foreign countries that extracts the income of the rich (Soak the Rich) would become an evil tax that extracts the blood of the poor (Soak the Poor) in China. Therefore, it is hoped that the authorities will start income tax at present to plant the foundation of wartime finance, but should still be treated as normal. The content should not be too harsh. (3) Chen Xing on economic problems in extraordinary times, conducted research on the preparation of manpower, financial resources, and material resources, and believed that the perseverance and outstanding spirit of the revival of Russia and Germany are worthy of our imitation. (4) Chen Changheng on several major economic issues and review of fiscal problems in the period of national crisis: First, he stated that there are three main elements of war: 1. People, 2. Finance, and 3. Machines. Our country has shortcomings in all of these. Next, he described in detail how to effectively supplement people and finance. In addition, the theses of Xiong Lingxiao, Wang Yutong, and others on finance in extraordinary times all advocated the collection of consumption and enjoyment taxes such as income tax and inheritance tax. Only Dong Xiujia's thesis on financial management strategies in extraordinary times did not advocate the adoption of tax increase policies that the people opposed too much, but suggested the expansion of paper currency and internal and external public debt policies that the people would not feel too much pain in the short term. Other theses by Zhu Qifu, Liu Fushu, etc. on the path that should be taken in agricultural finance and the problem of railway freight rates in extraordinary times are omitted.

Congratulatory Telegrams from Members

I imagine you all expounding great theories to save the times and benefit the people. I hereby congratulate you." (2) Ge Yufu in Jinan, transferred by Cao Lishun of Jiaotong University: "Zhaohuan, Guobao, Xulun, Zhihuan, and all attendees, greetings. I wish the annual meeting of our society progress and the prosperity of academic theory." (3) Xiao Chunjin in Nanchang, Jiangxi, transferred by Liu Dajun to the society: "Chunjin is unable to attend due to circumstances. I wish the annual meeting success and contribute to the construction of the national economy." (4) Mai Jianzeng, Director of the Guangzhou Finance Bureau: "I recently read in the newspaper that I am delighted to learn that our society is holding its twelfth annual meeting, with many talents gathering and each showing their expertise, and many effective constructions. I have returned south to Baiyue and hold a position in the city's finance. I am burdened with official duties and unable to attend, so I send a special congratulatory telegram."

Japanese Warships Arrive in Succession: Two More Arrived Yesterday Morning; Destroyer Staying in Shanghai, Transports Sailing Elsewhere; Carrying Over 300 Japanese Soldiers and Military Supplies 91

Yesterday morning, two more Japanese warships arrived in Shanghai. According to customs reports, one was the destroyer "No. 3," which entered the port at 4:40 AM, and the other was a transport ship, which entered the port at 9:25 AM. The destroyer docked at the Japanese Navy pontoon bridge at Lan Niddu, Pudong, while the transport ship docked at the Osaka Wharf in Yangshupu. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency witnessed at the time that the ship was crowded with people, unloading a large number of military supplies such as sacks, canvas, and ironware. A team of soldiers, either going up or down, was distributed on the side of the ship. Subsequently, the reporter continued to investigate in the afternoon and learned that the ship also carried about 380 Japanese soldiers, dressed in blue-black uniforms, who took more than a dozen trucks and successively entered the Jiangwan Japanese Marine Corps headquarters. After the ship unloaded the Japanese sailors and military supplies, it left Shanghai at about 4:00 PM and exited the Wusongkou at 5:10 PM. Its destination is unknown. However, another destroyer remains in Shanghai. It is not known whether the two ships came from Japan or other ports. As for the eight Japanese ships that arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, except for the three ships docked at the Osaka Wharf, which left at about 4:00 PM in the afternoon (some say they were moved to the Sanjia Water waters outside the Wusongkou), the four torpedoes were still docked at the Mitsui Wharf in Pudong yesterday. However, another giant ship docked at the Osaka Wharf also left the wharf at about 9:00 AM yesterday. Its destination is unknown. There are also two ships originally docked at the Japan Qing Company Wharf on Huangpu Road. Except for the flagship "Izumo" of the Third Fleet, which still remains there, one other ship, "Lotus," was also missing yesterday. In addition, the American gunboat "Asheville" also arrived in Shanghai yesterday.

Executive Yuan Has Issued an Order to Adopt National Goods Raincloth; Appropriate Handling of Increasing Tariff Rates on Foreign Goods; Ministry of Industry Notified the National Goods Association Yesterday 93

The Ministry of Industry notified the China National Goods Maintenance Association yesterday, stating, "The Executive Yuan previously delegated the association's request to clarify three points for distinguishing between national goods raincoats and lacquer cloths and non-national goods, requesting an order to adopt them, and to increase the import tariff rate on foreign goods raincoat cloths. It has been ordered to adopt them, and the Ministry of Finance has been consulted on the matter of increasing the import tariff rate on foreign goods raincoat cloths. The association has been notified of the case. The Ministry of Finance's Guanzi No. 30004 dated September 17, 25, stated, 'The Ministry of Industry's Gongzi No. 16514 dated July 20 of this year requested the China National Goods Maintenance Association to increase the import tariff rate on foreign goods raincoat cloths. Please check and handle the matter.' The Secretariat of the Executive Yuan also sent a letter to the ministry, which was handed over to the National Tariff Commission for investigation and reply. The ministry re-examined that the current lowest market price of foreign cotton raincoat cloth in Shanghai is about 40 cents per yard, and the cost is at most 30 cents per yard in national currency. The cost of domestic goods blank cloth is about 20 cents per yard, and the processing is at least 30 cents, totaling 50 cents. Compared with each other, the price of each yard of goods is already 10 cents apart, which proves that in the future, domestic goods raincoat cloth will have to strive to reduce costs in manufacturing in order to compete with foreign goods. As for the import tariff rate on foreign goods raincoat cloth, it has now been levied at 25% ad valorem. The matter of so-called raising the tariff rate should be re-examined and handled when the tariff rules are amended in the future. In addition to replying to the letter, it should be notified to your ministry for your reference." Special notification, Minister of Industry Wu Dingchang, September 26, 25th year of the Republic of China.

Expansion of the Shanghai-Hankou Line by Nisshin Causes Panic in Our Shipping Industry; Just as the Shipping Industry Slightly Recovers, Japanese Merchants Come to Compete with Us 95

The Nisshin Steamship Company has six commercial ships operating between Shanghai and Hankou: Yueyang, Ruiyang, Luoyang, Xiangyang, and Fengyang. In view of the flourishing cargo transportation between Shanghai and Hankou, the existing ships are not enough to operate. The company has now decided to add the two ships Dazhen and Daji starting from October 1. According to the shipping industry in this city, Nisshin's addition of commercial ships to operate on the Shanghai-Hankou line is intended to compete with the commercial ships on the Shanghai-Hankou line. However, it is not because of the development of business that they are adding ships. At a time when our country's shipping industry is slightly recovering, this move by Japanese merchants is indeed destroying the alliance sharing system. If measures are not taken to stop it urgently, the future of our shipping industry will inevitably be greatly affected.

Public Security Bureau Announces the Unveiling of the Xuan Sheng Case: Most of the Criminals are Notorious Repeat Offenders - Confessions of Mao and Wang 98

The Public Security Bureau's unveiling of the Xuan Sheng case, involving criminals Wang Zhensheng, Mao Yonghu, Zhao Yunhong, etc., has been briefly reported in previous news. The investigation of the case has concluded, and the entire case has been sent to the local court for trial. Now, the bureau publishes detailed information about the case, as recorded below:

Informant's Tip-Off

Since our bureau cracked down on Zhu Guisheng, Chen Enming, Jin Daoquan, and others in the Jiande Apartment last time for plotting to continue assassinating Japanese people, interrogation revealed that many key criminals involved in the assassination of Xuan Sheng were still at large. The Detective Brigade was immediately ordered to continue a rigorous investigation. Soon, a confidential informant reported that the criminals in this case were mostly notorious repeat offenders who had secretly discussed the matter at Zhao's house beforehand and distributed rewards at the Huashang Hotel afterward. The informant knew that these criminals often frequented the house of a Zhang family at No. 72 Shachang Street, Zhonghua Road, to plot their actions. Consequently, officers were dispatched with the informant to keep watch at the address, ready to capture them at the opportune moment.

Apprehension of the Criminals

The officers waited until 7:00 PM on the 25th of this month when they saw Mao Yonghu approaching slowly. As he neared the entrance of No. 72, they immediately stepped forward, apprehended him, and took him to the bureau. Meanwhile, they continued to wait. The next day (i.e., the 26th), Wang Zhensheng was captured at the bureau. According to Mao's confession, another criminal, Wang Zhensheng, was hiding at No. 10 Bao'an Branch Road. Thus, on the evening of the 27th, at 10:00 PM, they went to ask Zhang Rongfu's wife at No. 72 Shachang Street. After obtaining the information, they rushed to arrest him around 11:00 PM that night. Zhang was out and hadn't returned, so his wife, Zhang Ma's, was detained at the bureau for strict questioning. She confessed that Wang had moved to No. 46 Gongkuanli, Yangjiabang Road. They then escorted her to point out the location, and Wang and his wife, Wang Wang's, were arrested and taken to the bureau. This is a general account of the apprehension of the criminals at the time.

Main Points of the Interrogation

According to Mao Yonghu's confession, on June 26th or 27th of this year, he met with Li Ruiwu at Zhao Yunhong's house. Li said he wanted to kill an enemy and would pay 200 yuan to anyone willing to do it. At the time, I even helped him find someone to do it. Later, I found Wang Zhensheng, who was willing to do it, and accompanied him to Zhao's house to negotiate with Li. We also went to North Sichuan Road to look at the enemy. Li pointed out a Japanese person walking on the road, and that's when we knew we were going to kill a Japanese person. At the time, Wang Zhensheng said it wasn't convenient to act there. So the next day, I, Wang, and Li went to Qimei Road to scout the area. Li and Wang both said that this place was a good place to strike. So on July 4th, I went to Zhao's house, and Li immediately gave me ten yuan, telling me to go with Wang to check out No. 10 Bao'an Branch Road, Qimei Road. I paid five yuan for the rental fee. On July 5th, Wang Zhensheng and his wife moved from No. 71 Shachang Street, Nanshi, to No. 10 Bao'an Branch Road, Qimei Road. The next day (i.e., July 6th), Li told me to go with Wang to Qimei Road to check out the situation. So I went with Wang for a walk around the area. On the 7th, Li gave me a six-round revolver, a few bullets, I didn't pay attention. I gave the gun to Wang Zhensheng. Around 8:00 PM that evening, Wang and I went to near the intersection of Disiwei Road and Qihua Road and stood on opposite sides. We saw a Japanese couple walking by. Wang immediately tried to shoot, but he pulled the trigger several times, and it wouldn't fire. The Japanese people were frightened and ran away. On the 8th, Li sent another White Langlin pistol and a few bullets. I didn't see it clearly either and handed it over to Wang again. Around 8:00 PM that evening, Wang and I went to the old spot at the intersection of Disiwei Road and Qimei Road to wait. Soon, we saw a Japanese person walking by, and he tried to shoot again, but it wouldn't fire. On July 10th, Li gave me another revolver, six bullets. That evening, around 8:00 PM, Wang and I stood under a small tree opposite the ice cream stand on Qimei Road. Coincidentally, a Japanese person wearing Japanese clothes, holding a child in his arms, with another child following behind, walked from north to south, from Qimei Road to the Dongyang Garden on Disiwei Road. About ten minutes later, this Japanese person came out of the garden again, walking from south to north. At that time, Wang followed behind the Japanese person, about four or five steps apart, and then fired the gun, hitting the Japanese person, who fell to the ground. I fled towards Disiwei Road and immediately returned to the Changfa Hotel in Dongxinqiao. Wang also fled back. I asked Wang, and Wang said he had hit him, and the gun was lost, etc.

Furthermore, according to Wang Zhensheng's confession, the situation was almost entirely consistent with Mao Yonghu's confession. He also admitted to the gun misfiring on the evenings of the 7th and 8th. However, regarding the events of the evening of the 10th, he said that Mao Yonghu took out the gun that Wang had hidden on his body, and then Mao fired the gun, hitting Xuan Sheng. Then he gave the gun back to Wang. Wang then fled east to Hujia Muqiao and buried the gun in the garbage heap under the bridge before fleeing back to the Changfa Hotel, etc. According to Wang Zhensheng, on the evenings of the 7th and 8th, Wang Zhensheng fired the gun, and on the evening of the 10th, Wang carried the gun on his person. It is implausible that Mao took the gun and fired it and then returned it to Wang. Therefore, Wang Zhensheng is undoubtedly the main culprit in this case. (It was verified that the incident on the evening of July 7th, when Mao and Wang were firing the gun near the intersection of Disiwei Road and Qimei Road, but it misfired and the Japanese person fled in shock, was likely the Kurimoto incident, but it was on the 6th and not the 7th (or the record may be incorrect).) Further investigation revealed that Zhao Yunhong's confession regarding the pre-arrangement was no different from Mao Yonghu's confession. Two days later, Zhao went to the Huashang Hotel, and Mao and Li Ruiwu also came. Li took out 200 yuan and gave it to Mao. Mao took out 100 yuan, saying he had to give it to another person. The remaining 100 yuan was given to Wang Zhensheng (50 yuan), Zhao Yunhong (10 yuan), and Mao kept 30 yuan for himself. A day later, Li Ruiwu introduced a man in a suit called the Chief of Staff to meet me in the French Park, and he gave me a lot of encouragement, etc. According to the previous arrestee Jin Daoquan, this so-called Chief of Staff was actually Hua Kezhi. Furthermore, the main culprit in this case, Wang Zhensheng, is Mao Yonghu's sworn brother, and Mao's father is Zhao Yunhong's apprentice. Zhao was entrusted by Li Ruiwu, and Li was acting under the secret orders of Hua Kezhi. Therefore, the mastermind behind this case is undoubtedly Hua Kezhi.

Retrieval of the Gun and Inspection

Based on the confession of the main culprit Wang Zhensheng, the next morning (the 18th), at around 7:00 AM, officers were dispatched with Wang to Hujia Muqiao, where they retrieved the gun from the mud in the garbage heap under the bridge. A film was taken. Then, officers were dispatched to the Public Concession Police Station's gun examination room to examine the gun. It was verified that the gun was a .32 caliber, American-made, six-chamber revolver, brand name Smith & Wesson. It was also found that in the six chambers, five chambers still contained five unfired bullets, and one chamber contained one fired cartridge case. The chamber with the cartridge case was in the center of the firing pin, so it could be determined that it was the chamber from which the shot was fired. It can also be determined that only one shot was fired, and the trigger was only pulled once. However, the bullets in the gun were all French-made F.N. brand automatic pistol steel-jacketed bullets, not the original bullets for the revolver. It can be determined that the intention was to reduce the sound of the explosion when fired, to avoid the attention of passersby, and to confuse the police so that it would be difficult to identify the type of gun used. It was also found that the four numbers etched on the outside of the gun barrel had been filed off in advance, and the marks of the file were still faintly visible. However, they did not know that there was a number etched on the inside of the gun barrel, which had not been erased. This proves that the criminals in this case had a very tight organization and had considered it carefully before acting, which is completely different from ordinary assassinations. After test firing, the traces of the rifling on the bullet head, the spiral lines on the bottom of the cartridge case, and the firing pin marks were compared meticulously with the bullet head taken from Xuan Sheng's head in the hospital and the traces of the rifling and spiral lines and the firing pin marks on the cartridge case taken from the gun chamber this time. They were identical, without any difference. Therefore, it can be determined that the bullet head taken from Xuan Sheng's head was fired from that gun (17 inspection photos have been submitted to the court).

Conclusion of the Case

After the arrest of Mao and Zhao, Jin Daoquan and others were sent back to our bureau by the police. Jin was immediately brought to face Mao and Zhao, and both sides confessed that they knew each other, but Mao and Zhao called Jin "Little Wang" and "Old Three." Jin also admitted that when Liu Laosi introduced him to Mao and Zhao, he referred to him as Wang Laosan. However, Mao and Zhao also pointed out that the person who introduced them was Li Ruiwu, and the descriptions of Liu and Li's appearance and the number of times Liu (i.e., Li) brought Jin to meet Mao and Zhao were completely identical. Therefore, it was known that Liu Laosi was an alias for Li Ruiwu. From this, it can be seen that the secret organization led by Hua Kezhi is completely no different from the Communist Party organization. There is only a vertical relationship and no horizontal relationship. The strictness can be imagined. Furthermore, the descriptions of the assassination of Xuan Sheng given by the arrestees in this case are the same as the descriptions of Zhang Shimin's leading Zhu Guisheng et al. to assassinate Nakayama Hideo given by the criminals Zhu Guisheng and Chen Enming arrested by our bureau last time in the Jiande Apartment, and the descriptions of Hua Kezhi's leading Zhu Guisheng, Jin Daoquan, Chen Enming et al. to plot to continue assassinating Japanese people given by Jin Daoquan. The intention and strategy are exactly the same. Furthermore, Zhang Shimin and Hua Kezhi are both Wang Yaqiao's top cadres. From this, it can be clearly shown that the previous assassinations of Japanese people were a consistent sabotage policy of Wang Yaqiao's reactionary organization. As a result of our bureau's efforts to investigate each case, we have fully understood the location of their conspiracy. Therefore, for the sake of eliminating the source of chaos for the party and the country, for the sake of consolidating the security of this city, and for the sake of the safety of the lives and property of Chinese and foreign people, we will further collaborate with the police authorities of the concessions to rigorously search for and arrest the remnants of the reactionary organization, in order to completely eliminate such ominous events.

Customs Recruitment of Marine Engineers: Age Limit Issue 103

The Chinese Marine Engineers Association sent a letter to the Inspector General of Customs of the Jianghai Customs requesting a modification of the age limit for marine engineers. The original letter stated: "Respectfully, we recently read in the newspaper that your department's marine vessel section plans to recruit many marine engineers, in order to select talents to benefit customs affairs. The intention is far-reaching and admirable. However, there seems to be room for discussion regarding the age limit. Our association takes the liberty of requesting a slight increase. If the limit could be set at 22 to 40 years old, it would be more appropriate. Our association has more than a thousand members with extensive service experience, which can be said to be abundant. However, the average age is over 30 and around 40, which is very different from your department's limit. We are sending this letter specifically, hoping that you will make accommodations to show fairness. Furthermore, we hope that equal emphasis will be placed on academic knowledge and experience in the exam subjects. We sincerely hope for your consideration and reply to our humble request and maintain our public friendship."

Ministry of Finance Orders Salt Authority to Implement New Salt Law: Starting with Lianghuai and Other Salt Fields, Zhejiang Salt Fields May Be Difficult to Implement Immediately 104

Since the Legislative Yuan passed the new Salt Law last October, the Salt Authority has been actively rectifying various provincial salt fields, improving field production, and preventing tax evasion. However, China's salt affairs have long-standing problems, such as the private merchant allocation system, which is difficult to abolish immediately. Therefore, the implementation of the new Salt Law is not easy. The prerequisite is to rectify the salt fields. Currently, the salt fields in various provinces that have achieved concrete success in rectification are Shandong, Lianghuai, and Changlu, while the rectification project in Zhejiang, except for salt fields in Yuyao and other places, cannot be completed within the year. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance ordered the Salt Authority to implement the new Salt Law in stages by region. The first places to implement the new Salt Law will be the Changlu, Shandong, and Lianghuai salt fields. The implementation of tax collection and free trade can begin in November. However, the implementation of the new Salt Law in the Zhejiang salt fields may not be realized in the short term. As for the implementation of the new Salt Law in Liangguang, it is still pending.

Amidst the Currency Reform in France, the French Exchange Rate Hits an Unprecedented Low: A Continuing Downward Trend, China is Less Affected 105

In order to prevent capital flight, the French government is implementing a new currency policy, devaluing the French franc, and abolishing the gold standard. After the gold was nationalized, the international exchange rate was greatly shaken. All related countries have taken new measures to cope with the situation. Since China's exports to France are limited, it is less affected. The details are recorded as follows:

Bank of China Nominal Price

On the morning of the 28th, the Bank of China's quoted exchange rate was 582 French francs per 100 national currency units, which was a nominal price, not an actual transaction price. Compared with the closing price of 464.25 French francs on Saturday, it was a decrease of 118 French francs, which can be described as an unprecedented drop. The exchange rates of other countries, such as London at 1 shilling and 2.5 pence, New York at 30 gold dollars, Berlin at 76 marks, Japan at 103 yen, and Hong Kong at 97 Hong Kong dollars, remained the same as last week, with no change. According to economic experts, based on the current international trend, the value of the French franc may continue to decline. It will only gradually stabilize after the French government officially announces the new currency law.

Gold Price Rises Again

Yesterday, the gold market rose sharply again. The opening price in the morning was 1155 yuan, a sharp increase of 14.3 yuan compared to last Saturday (the day before). The buying interest was still high, and it once rose to outside the 60 yuan mark. The fluctuation was more than 10 yuan within a few minutes. The closing price in the morning was 1156.7 yuan, an increase of 1.7 yuan. After the opening in the afternoon, it soared, and the opening price was 1157.8 yuan. The buying momentum was still rising, and it immediately rose outside the 60 yuan mark, and the highest price was 1163.3 yuan. It then fell slightly to 1157.1 yuan. As a result, the closing price was 1161.7 yuan. The increase was 6.7 yuan for the day, a huge increase of 21 yuan compared to last week.

The items that have not been inspected will be transported to Beijing for continued inspection. Once all the antiquities have been transported, the Shanghai office will be closed, and all staff will be transferred back to the museum to work. After the antiquities are transported to Beijing, a portion will be selected for display.

Improving Passenger Transport Order: Completely For the Sake of Passengers, Cleanliness and Safety are Taken Care Of 109

The Ministry of Railways believes that the perfection of passenger transport order on each route is of great importance to the reputation and business prospects of the railway. To remind service personnel on each route, ten items for improving passenger transport order have been listed and ordered to be followed by all bureaus and their subordinates. After receiving the order, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus have printed the ten key points and distributed them to all stations along the two routes for unified implementation. The following is an excerpt. (1) Ticket sales: Stations with heavy passenger traffic will sell tickets all day. (2) Passenger ticket purchase order: Proceed in order to avoid crowding. (3) Passenger boarding order: Get off first, then get on, to avoid congestion in the carriage. (4) Take care of passenger seats: Arrange passenger seats and luggage carefully. (5) Strictly check tickets: Strictly enforce ticket checks at the station and on the train, but do not disturb the peace of passengers. (6) Ticket inspection attitude: Be respectful in words and deal with situations peacefully. (7) Train attendant calls station names: When the train arrives at the station, call out the station name to prevent passengers from overshooting the station. (8) Maintain cleanliness: Strive for cleanliness at the station and on the train to enhance the appearance and hygiene. (9) Baggage check-in: Pay attention to whether baggage is checked in at any time and expedite the process to avoid long waits for passengers. (10) Baggage safety: No one is allowed to enter or exit the baggage room and baggage car. Train attendants should do their best to take care of passengers' carry-on baggage.

Cheng Linsheng and Nephew Accused of Forging Leases to Conceal Assets – Rootai Factory’s Annual Rent Only 4,000 Yuan, While the Lease Term Extends to 20 Years – Creditors Deem It Absolutely Suspicious 114

Cheng Linsheng, a wealthy businessman from Shexian, Huizhou, who made his fortune in real estate in Shanghai, and his nephew, Yi Ze, founded the Rootai United Flour Mill. Due to business failure and mounting debts, the Cheng family gathered creditors in the past to discuss a plan to repay all debts in installments and continue operations. Unexpectedly, the factory was suddenly leased to Hu Xiannan from Shexian, who added the characters "Yi Ji" to the brand name to distinguish it. This leasing behavior dissatisfied creditors, leading to numerous lawsuits against the Cheng family. Now, De Tai Yun Ji Industrial Raw Materials Company, a creditor of the factory, claims that Yun Qing, due to Rootai owing them over 21,000 yuan in goods, obtained a court judgment for repayment. When applying to the court for enforcement and seizure of the factory, Hu Xiannan stepped forward to object. Therefore, Zhang accused Hu of colluding with the Cheng family to forge leases, conceal assets, and harm creditors. He filed a criminal self-lawsuit in the First Special District Local Court against the two Chengs and Hu, stating that the Rootai factory’s assets are worth 200,000 yuan, and its annual profit is 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. However, the lease contract with Hu Xiannan specifies an annual rent of only 4,000 yuan and a term as long as 20 years. It is as if the two Chengs are willing to gift Hu an annual surplus of 50,000 to 60,000 yuan. If this had nothing to do with the creditors' rights, private gifts would not be prohibited by law. However, with this contract in place, all the factory’s assets, business, customers, trademarks, etc., are bound by the 20-year fake lease. When auctioned, no one will likely inquire, making enforcement impossible. As a result, the Cheng family's debt to the plaintiff will be completely unrecoverable and seized by Hu. If there were no fake lease, only half a year's profit from the factory would be sufficient to repay the plaintiff's debt. Now, using the fake lease as a smokescreen, they are completely concealing the factory's assets and profits, which is extremely illegal. Furthermore, Hu is originally a retainer of the Cheng family, lacking both the funds and experience to run a factory. Yet, he appears to sign the lease. Their plan to jointly forge, conceal assets, harm the plaintiff's creditors, and share the spoils is self-evident, fitting the descriptions in Articles 211, 356, and 28 of the Criminal Law. Therefore, it is specifically requested that the court review and approve the summons of the three defendants for punishment according to law. Moreover, according to Hu Xiannan's objection in another case, he admitted to earning a daily surplus of 156 yuan. Based on this calculation, his monthly income is 4,680 yuan. Hu has been operating Rootai with a false lease, continuing business for 17 months, obtaining an illegal profit of 79,560 yuan. He should be ordered to return a portion of it to sufficiently repay the plaintiff's debt, punishing the deceitful and protecting rights, etc. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng Shide conducted the trial. Both Chengs avoided appearing in court, but Hu arrived with his defense lawyer, Li Lin. The plaintiff's lawyer, Chen Ming, presented the reasons for the lawsuit and submitted all evidence to question the defendant. Hu claimed that he continued to trade with the plaintiff after leasing the factory, and the plaintiff initially had no questions, firmly denying the forgery of the lease. The court adjourned the hearing to investigate further and retry the case later.

Around the Mid-Autumn Festival in the Lunar Calendar, the Tidal Surge in the Huangpu River Was Not High – It Will Not Overflow the Banks Unless There Is Wind and Rain – Recent Situation of the Dredging of the Shuntan Shoal 115

According to a Datong News Agency reporter's inquiry with the Huangpu Conservancy Bureau yesterday, the dangerous period for the autumn flood tide in the Huangpu River has passed. Although there will still be several days of high tide at the beginning of the month, the levels will be lower than last month, unaffected by weather, and not worth noting. The details are recorded below:

Huangpu River High Tide Period Passed

According to a Datong News Agency reporter's inquiry with the Huangpu Conservancy Bureau, although the 3rd of next month is the 18th day of the eighth lunar month, traditionally believed to be a day of significant tidal surge, the Bureau predicts that the highest tides on that day will occur at 1:39 AM (predicted at 11 feet 1 inch) and 10:59 PM (predicted at 11 feet 3 inches). Compared to the high tides of last month, these are lower. Therefore, if there is no bad weather or strong winds and heavy rain, there is no fear of the tide reaching the shore.

Current Status of the Dredging of the Shuntan Shoal

The Datong News Agency reporter also learned that since the Bureau dispatched the "Construction" dredging vessel to dredge the Shuntan Shoal outside the Wusongkou, 5 million tons of sediment have been dredged. Once the second dredging vessel is completed and joins the dredging efforts, the initial dredging work (deepening the depth from 17 feet at low tide to 26 feet) can be completed within five years. This will allow heavily loaded ships to enter and exit the Wusongkou without obstruction, significantly contributing to the prosperity of Shanghai's commerce.

Leather Goods Guild Notice: Members Required to Join by Deadline 116

The Shanghai Leather Goods Industry Guild issued a notice yesterday to all leather goods manufacturers in the city, stating: This notice concerns membership. Since its establishment, the Guild has been active for several months, and membership enrollment has been enthusiastic. It has come to our attention that some manufacturers, misunderstanding the law and the organizational procedures of the Industry Guild Law, have attempted to organize their own industry guilds, submitting three applications that have been repeatedly rejected by the Municipal Party Headquarters. Now, the Guild has repeatedly sent personnel to solicit membership from those manufacturers, but they have all cited reasons such as "Golden Fortune," "Thai Abundance," "Mainland," and others also planning to organize guilds, using these as excuses to delay and refuse to join. This behavior not only hinders the Guild's work but also violates the law. Therefore, we specifically notify all leather goods manufacturers to promptly come to the Guild within seven days to fill out application forms and join the Guild to comply with the law. Please do not delay. Otherwise, the Guild will have no choice but to comply with the instructions of higher authorities and take legal action.

Tragedy of Husband Killing After Wife's Adultery: Paramour Fled with Knife Wound, Woman Seriously Injured 121

He Ruichen, a 41-year-old Shandong native, has been selling fruit for a living. Fifteen years ago, he married He Xie, also from his hometown, and they lived together at 797 Qu Zhenren Road in Nanshi, raising a daughter who is now 13 years old. Unexpectedly, He Xie recently became restless and had an affair with Dong Xiyuan from Shandong. On the 14th of this month, she eloped with Dong, taking with her over 80 yuan in property, and they lived together at 1398 Yutong Lane, Robert Road in western Shanghai, as if they were husband and wife. After his wife's elopement, He Ruichen searched everywhere. On the 20th of this month, he encountered Dong Xiyuan, his wife's paramour, in Zhabei, and they argued, followed by a physical fight. Dong was stabbed with small scissors by He at the time. They were both handed over to the Public Security Bureau. Because the matter involved abduction and injury, they were transferred to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office for investigation. Due to insufficient evidence, the prosecutor ordered both parties to be dismissed without prosecution. Later, He Ruichen twisted Dong's younger brother, Dong Xixiu, and brought him to the Ximen Public Security Bureau, providing Dong Xiyuan's hiding place. Detective Lian Mingsheng, accompanied by Dong Xixiu, went to the Putuo Road Police Station to request assistance on the day before yesterday. The head of the police station dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to 1398 Yutong Lane, Robert Road. As expected, they saw Dong Xiyuan and He Xie lying in the same bed. They were both taken to the police station. Although He Xie admitted to adultery with Dong, she pointed out that He Ruichen was not her official husband either, only having a cohabitation relationship. The police station immediately ordered He Ruichen to provide formal marriage certificates. However, he was unable to provide them at the time, so Dong and He Xie were released by the police station at around 8 a.m. on the morning before yesterday. They hired two rickshaws and returned to their home in Yutong Lane. Unexpectedly, He Ruichen, at that time, stole a kitchen knife from the Wang family at 1398 Yutong Lane and hid a bayonet. He ambushed at the entrance of the alley. Upon seeing Dong arrive, he rushed forward with the kitchen knife and slashed twice. Dong dodged the first strike, but the second strike hit Dong's right wrist. Dong fled in pain. Upon seeing this, He Xie hurriedly got out of the rickshaw and fled, but He caught up and stabbed her several times in the right arm and chest with the bayonet he had hidden. She fell to the ground with serious injuries. Chinese policeman No. 2482 arrived, took the injured to the hospital separately, and took He, along with the two murder weapons, to the Putuo Road Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the 8th Criminal Court of the First Special Court. The police lawyer, Zhang Tianyin, charged him with attempted murder under Article 271, Section 2 of the Criminal Law, and theft under Article 320, presenting the case. He said that He Xie was seriously injured and is currently in the hospital. He requested that the hearing be postponed. According to Dong Xiyuan, he admitted to having an affair with He Xie for only a few days and described the circumstances of being stabbed by the defendant. When questioned, He Ruichen admitted to the assault. Judge Huang Risheng reviewed the confessions and ordered the defendant to be detained for a retrial next Tuesday.

Fujian Native Association Contacts Compatriots at Home and Abroad to Promote Economic Construction in Fujian Province 122

The Fujian Native Association in Shanghai, realizing that the national situation is becoming increasingly dangerous and that rural Fujian Province is bankrupt, believes that there is no way to save the country and survive without starting with economic construction. Therefore, it was decided at the sixth standing committee meeting to send letters to compatriots at home and abroad to jointly seek the welfare of their hometown and promote economic construction in Fujian Province. It is reported that the content of the letter is quite important. It is recorded below: Our Fujian Province is near the sea, and transportation is convenient. In the past, during the closed-door era, Fujian merchants' footprints spread all over the north and south of the country. After the opening of ports, Shanghai rose as a major trading port. Fellow countrymen from Jiangsu and Ningbo successively moved to Shanghai, but each established their own organizations. There are Quanzhang Guild Hall, Jinhui Guild Hall, and Xing'an Guild Hall in southern Fujian. There are Sanshan and Funing Guild Hall in eastern Fujian, and Shayong Public Office in northern Fujian. There are also organizations such as Yongding Guild Hall in western Fujian. They are not connected to each other, and their ability to act externally is weak. Their benefit to their fellow countrymen is inevitably limited. Since the restoration, more and more villagers have arrived, but they are still scattered. Those who know this are worried and urgently advocate the establishment of the Fujian Native Association in Shanghai to unite their friendship. Many fellow countrymen have expressed their support, and it was established. Up to now, more than a dozen general meetings have been convened. The officials of each session are respectful of their hometown and have worked hard to learn and plan. The scale is roughly in place. When refugees were stranded in Shanghai and could not return home, the association would verify the facts and send them back to their hometown. If they were deceived and had no way to appeal, they would also do their best to help them. Other good deeds, such as resolving difficulties and helping the poor, are all done together. Not only that, but in the past, when the military departments were rampant and arbitrarily increased troops, the association was deeply concerned that the more troops stationed, the heavier the burden on the people of Fujian. Together with the Fujian Governor, they prevented the troop recruitment ships from passing through Shanghai and actively negotiated with the shipping companies to prevent them from being transported to Fujian. This not only protects the legal rights and interests of the fellow countrymen in Shanghai but also reduces the suffering of all the fellow countrymen in Fujian. When the National Revolutionary Army launched the Northern Expedition and established the capital in Nanjing, more and more villagers came and went, and the association's position became even more important than before. Moreover, at a time when strong neighbors are watching us like tigers and dangers abound, if we stick to old rules and do not seek to unite, we will not be able to save the country and survive. Therefore, in the summer of this year, we decided to revise the constitution, re-establish the plan, expand the solicitation of members, and raise funds to support various public welfare undertakings and the economic construction of our Fujian Province. In recent months, we have divided into teams to solicit members. Thanks to the efforts of fellow countrymen in persuading and raising funds, the results have been considerable. However, this matter is of great importance, and it will not be successful without the joint efforts of everyone. We hope that fellow countrymen at home and abroad will join us in this great endeavor. Whether it is an organization or an individual, we welcome everyone to participate. You have always been concerned about the country and enthusiastic about public welfare, and you have been admired by fellow countrymen everywhere. If you would check the second article and the second item of the fourth article of the association's constitution and approve joining as a special director or special member of the association, we would be able to maintain permanent contact, jointly seek to save our hometown, and consolidate the foundation of the association. This would not only be a blessing for the fellow countrymen in Shanghai but also a blessing for the entire Fujian Province.

Cao went inside and, seeing that the owner and apprentices were tied up, untied them and learned of the robbery. He reported the situation to the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched Chinese detectives Wang Runhe and Zhang Faxiang to investigate. Around 9:00 PM the night before last, they learned that the bandits Wu Xiaosheng, Chen Donggui from Zhenjiang, Wang Agen from Anhui, and Wang Haiquan from Changzhou were hiding in Room 12 of the Wuzhou Inn at 10 Guangdong Road. They secretly went with Western detectives and arrested the four, and also detained three suspects in Room 14: Zhang Agen from Changzhou, Tang Axi from Wuxi, and Yu Agen. They confessed that their accomplice, Chen Ronglong from Jiangbei, was staying at the Lao De and Xiao Inn on Maimaquelo Road in the French Concession. They went with detectives from the French Concession Police Station and arrested Chen, and brought them all back to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Zhang Shizhu, a lawyer from the Municipal Council, stated the case and said that Zhang Agen, Tang Axi, Yu Agen, and Chen Ronglong were not involved in the Huadong Shoe Store robbery, but had committed multiple theft cases in the Concession. He asked for an extension to investigate further. Then, the Chinese and Western detectives reported the process of arresting the defendants. They presented the ropes that were used to bind the apprentices at the time of the robbery. Only Ding Longhai, an apprentice from the Huadong Shoe Store, appeared in court and testified about the robbery. When questioned, the defendants gave evasive answers. Judge Zhong Qing ordered that they be remanded in custody for further investigation.

Letter to the Editor 141

To the Editor: I have read in the news section of your newspaper on the 18th of this month regarding the Lu Clan Ancestral Hall and the investigation of public property, which mentioned Lu Daocui and Li Tixian colluding in illegal sales. Lu Daocui transferred the land in the Yangjing District to me in 1934, and I sold it to the Song family the following year. These were all formal transactions, with the transfer registered at the Land Bureau and a land ownership certificate transferred as proof. It is evident that what is reported in your newspaper is inconsistent with the facts. I believe that your reporter relied on the contents of the lawsuit filed by Lu Zhiqing for registration, and I am deeply concerned that the outside world, not knowing the actual details, may mistakenly believe it to be true, which would harm my reputation. I am writing to request a correction. Sincerely, Li Tixian, September 26.

The designated schools and drill materials are transcribed as follows:

Designated Schools

Jingye Middle School, 150 male students; Wuben Girls' Middle School, 150 female students; Dagong Vocational School, 100 male students; Muli Girls' Middle School, 150 female students; Municipal Chamber of Commerce Vocational School, 100 male students; Junyi Middle School, 150 male students; Qingxin Girls' Middle School, 100 female students; Kaiming Middle School, 100 male students; Aiguo Girls' Middle School, 150 female students; Private Shanghai Middle School, 150 male students; Shanghai Kindergarten Normal School, 150 female students; Minzhi Middle School, 100 male students; Jianguo Middle School, 150 male students; Qixiu Girls' Middle School, 100 female students; Chongde Girls' Middle School, 100 female students; Guangdong East Middle School, 100 male students; Hujiang Affiliated Middle School, 150 male students; Yuqing Middle School, 100 male students; Fudan Experimental Middle School, 150 male students; Xinmin Middle School, 100 male students; Qiude Girls' Middle School, 150 female students; Chengzhong Middle School, 150 male students; Youth Middle School, 100 male students; Huadong Girls' Middle School, 100 female students.

Drill Materials

Section 1: Limb Exercise, (1) Left foot steps out to the side, both arms lift to the side, (2) Raise heels, both arms lift to the upper side, (3) Return to position (1), (4) Left foot, both arms return to original position, (5) (6) (7) (8) Switch to right foot stepping out to the side, a total of 32 beats. Section 2: Chest Lifting Exercise, both arms lifted forward horizontally, (2) Expand both arms to the left and right, palms upward, while lifting the chest, (3) Return to position (1), (4) Arms return to original position, (5) (6) (7) (8) Same as above, a total of 32 beats. Section 3: (1) Arms flexed sideways, jumping with feet apart, (2) Bend upper body forward while stretching arms forward (downward), (3) Return to position 1, (4) Return to original position, (5) (6) (7) (8) Same as above, a total of 32 beats. Section 4: Body Rotation Exercise, preparation: feet apart, fists clenched, elbows flexed horizontally at the waist in a hugging position, (1) Upper body rotates to the left, while the right fist punches out to the left with the back of the hand facing up (arm and hand), upper body returns to center, right fist retracts, (3) Upper body rotates to the left, while the left fist punches out to the right, (4) Upper body returns to center, left fist retracts, (5) (6) (7) (8) Same as above, a total of 32 beats, return to standing position on the last beat. Section 5: Waist Exercise, (1) Both hands on waist, left foot steps out to the left (arrow step), (2) Body leans to the left, (3) Body returns to straight position, (4) Left and right foot retract, put hands down, (5) Both hands on waist, right foot steps out to the right (arrow step), (6) Body leans to the right, (7) Upper body returns to straight position, (8) Right foot retracts, a total of 32 beats. Section 6: (1) Feet apart jump, while both arms lift to the side, (2) Return to original position, repeat as above for a total of 32 beats. Section 7: Breathing Exercise, (1) (2) Arms lift upward from the front, inhale, (3) (4) Arms drop downward from the side, exhale, (5) (6) (7) (8) Same as above, a total of 16 beats.

On the World Games Delegation - Letter No. 15, Special Correspondent Feng Youzhen 150

(7)(3) Modern Pentathlon

(7)(4) Solemn and Grand Closing Ceremony

The Games, which opened on August 1st, proceeded smoothly for half a month, until the 16th, when all events were successfully completed, and a solemn and grand closing ceremony was held. The Games venue had been quiet for a long time after the end of the track and field events. On the 16th, in the afternoon, it became lively again due to the equestrian competition. More than 100,000 spectators were present from morning to night, without a break. German Chancellor Hitler, along with dignitaries from various countries, entered the venue at 5 PM and did not leave until after the closing ceremony was completed at 9:30 PM. The closing ceremony was originally scheduled to begin at 7 PM, but was delayed due to the late finish of the equestrian competition. It officially began at 8:45 PM with a 300-person orchestra playing powerful music. More than 20 searchlights were specially prepared around the venue, simultaneously emitting a deep blue light, focusing on the upper room of the venue. The entire venue was shrouded in such a mysterious color, which could not help but create a solemn feeling. At 8:50 PM, each of the 51 countries participating in the Games sent one representative, holding their national flag, to enter the venue from the west gate. The order of procession was the opposite of that at the opening ceremony. The flag bearer for our country was boxing athlete Xi Guidi. Amidst the enthusiastic cheers of the audience, the representatives of each country walked to the rostrum and lined up in a row. The president of the Games, Mr. Latour, walked from the rostrum to the microphone in the center of the venue and gave a brief closing speech. After the speech, 51 uniformed young women took flower wreaths and hung them on the flagpoles of each country. At the same time, 2,000 young men and women sang the Games anthem in unison. The Games flag was also slowly lowered amidst the sound of saluting cannons. The representatives of each country then walked out of the venue through the gate below the rostrum. At the same time, the bells rang, and the flame that had been burning for half a month was extinguished. The Games flag was carried by five uniformed staff members to the rostrum, and then escorted by eight samurai holding swords to the broadcasting platform. The mayor of Los Angeles, USA, the host city of the previous Games, officially handed it over to the mayor of Berlin for safekeeping. At the same time, the president of the Games announced that the next Games would be held in Tokyo. The flagpole on the sign raised the flags of Greece, the host country of the first Games, Germany, the host country of this Games, and Japan, the host country of the next Games. After the flags of the three countries were lowered, the glorious 11th World Games officially came to a close amidst the singing of the German national anthem by the entire audience.

(7)(5) Thoughts on Participating in the Games

The Games have come to a successful conclusion, and athletes from various countries have returned home one after another. This time, our country sent more than 100 representatives, traveling tens of thousands of miles, in a grand manner to participate in the Games. As a result, the entire army was wiped out and returned in a miserable defeat. As a reporter who personally experienced the situation, I was deeply moved and had indescribable feelings.

Regarding the health of the people, the representatives our country sent this time can be said to be the elite of the country. However, when they entered this world arena and compared themselves with athletes from various countries, the disparity in skills was vast, and the inferiority in physical fitness was shocking. No matter which arena, as soon as our athletes were compared with others, one could immediately feel that the others were so tall and strong, while we were so short and weak. The outcome of the competition could be predicted without even competing. For example, in the China-England football match, the skills of our players were by no means inferior to those of England. The result of the first half was as expected, without conceding a goal. However, after 45 minutes of intense battle, the players showed signs of fatigue, and they lost two goals in the second half and were eliminated. Therefore, the outcome of this football match was not judged on the merits of skill, but on the strength of physical fitness. Regarding the basketball game, the physical fitness of our players was not only far inferior to that of strong teams such as the United States and Canada, but also inferior to that of Japan. Wang Yuzeng's height cannot be considered short, but the Japanese center was half a head taller than him. The physical fitness of the other players was also far inferior to others. The situation on the track and field was even more obvious. Jia Lianren participated in the 1,500-meter preliminary, and he ran well in the first three laps, competing fiercely with famous players from various countries without showing any weakness. However, in the last lap, others were able to sprint forward with ease, while he was exhausted and fell behind. Chen Baoqiu, a shot put athlete, is known as the "Iron Ox" and has the most robust figure among all athletes. However, when mixed with the iron oxen from various countries, one could almost suspect that he had turned into a mud ox. The situation of the other team members can be imagined. In short, our country's participation in this Games was a complete defeat in terms of skills, which is certainly a national shame, but the inferiority in physical fitness should be regarded as a crisis for the nation. We should determine the direction of sports in the future. We should not only train many excellent athletes, but also pay attention to the future of the nation and strengthen everyone's health.

Regarding technical training, we cannot win honor for the country in this Games, and we will inevitably be completely defeated. This was something that was expected before going abroad. We cannot blame our coaches, nor can we blame our athletes. However, we must not attribute this failure to an inevitable result and dismiss it. We must take this complete defeat as the supreme shame of the country and the nation. We cannot always be willing to succumb. We must strive to make progress in technology and raise our eyebrows and exhale for the country in the next Games. Otherwise, we are weak and shameless. The international sports arena is as snobbish as the international political arena. At the opening ceremony on August 1st, when our athletes marched in, the momentum and the neat formation were no weaker than any other country. However, the film taken by Germany did not have the shadow of our delegation because they simply did not take China seriously. We should regard this as a national shame, just as we have been invaded by others. When the results of each competition were announced in the Games venue, the flagpoles on the wooden signs raised the flags of the top three winners, and the orchestra played the national anthem of the champion. We often heard more than 100,000 spectators singing the powerful and inspiring German national anthem along with the music, and we couldn't help but feel awe. We also saw the flags of the colonies of India and Egypt flying on the flagpoles in the center of the sign, and we couldn't help but feel ashamed. We couldn't see a shadow of China or hear a sound of China in the venue, and we should regard this as a national shame, just as we were being whipped. In short, we failed this time, but failure has its price, and failure has its lessons. We must learn our lessons from this failure, seize our price, and wash away our shame, unless we don't want to show our skills in the international arena again.

Regarding the spirit of the athletes, our athletes' participation in this Games was far inferior to others not only in terms of physical fitness and skills, but also in terms of spirit. None of the track and field athletes' results could catch up with their inherent strength. Although it is said that the fatigue of the journey and acclimatization are also important reasons, the lack of determination of the athletes is an undeniable fact. Especially the basketball team, after being defeated by the Japanese team in the first battle, their will was depressed, their spirits were scattered, and they almost disintegrated. When we look at the athletes from other countries, no matter what their strength is, their spirit of desperately fighting and not showing submission until the last second is truly admirable. Secondly, the sense of responsibility of our athletes should also be cultivated. Before the opening of the Games, the German starter, fearing that the athletes from various countries did not understand the German starting slogan, specially gathered the athletes from various countries participating in the race to practice starting and firing the gun. Athletes from various countries went to participate, but none of our athletes went. There were also one or two athletes who gave up participating in the event because they slept too late at night during the Games. These situations must be corrected. If we want to develop Chinese sports, in terms of athletes, we must cultivate the spirit of struggle and responsibility.

Regarding the organizational aspects, the scope of the World Games is so vast that it is difficult for those who have not personally experienced it to imagine. However, Germany managed it in an orderly manner, and the order was very good. In my previous communication, I used the eight characters "no one idle, no one without work" to describe the German's way of doing things, which is by no means an exaggeration. During the Games, no matter which part, we never saw an employee wearing a badge who was idle and had nothing to do, nor did we ever encounter a situation where we could not find someone to contact about something. But our delegation was different. The telephone at the Chinese office in the Olympic Village often rang for a long time without being answered. Athletes were sick, and no one cared about food. Even communist publications were repeatedly found in the village, and no one was taking action. With such a small organization, there are still so many flaws. Can we not be ashamed? I hope that after participating in this Games, the delegation can bring the German spirit of doing things back to the motherland. There are too many lessons that this Games has given us. There are really thousands of things to say, and I don't know where to start. I think if we can work together to transform the future of Chinese sports on the four points mentioned above, we can certainly embark on a bright path.

Education News

Overview of Implementing Free Education in the 24th Year of the Republic (3) 157

— Qinghai

Received a central subsidy of 80,000 yuan for free education. Due to the province's financial difficulties, it was unable to raise its own funds. There are more than 100,000 out-of-school children in the province. In the 24th year, 110 short-term primary schools were temporarily established. When the Ministry of Education sent personnel to inspect this year, the newly added short-term schools enrolled 8,648 children.

Beiping

Received a central subsidy of 45,000 yuan for free education and raised 80,000 yuan from the city. There are 96,296 out-of-school children in the city. The city plans to establish 480 grades of short-term primary schools in the 24th year. When the Ministry of Education sent personnel to inspect last time, it saw that only 90 grades had been established in the first semester and hoped that all grades that had not been established would be established in the second semester.

Tianjin

Received a central subsidy of 35,000 yuan for free education and originally planned to raise 120,000 yuan from the city, of which 10,000 yuan has been allocated successively. There are 80,000 out-of-school children. In the 24th year, it is planned to establish a two-part system of short-term primary schools and additional ordinary primary schools, with a total of 320 grades. Only 30 schools were established in the first semester, and the rest are planned to be added in the second semester. However, since funds cannot be allocated in full, it will be difficult to promote them as much as possible.

Shanghai

Received a central subsidy of 80,000 yuan for free education and originally planned to raise 90,000 yuan from the city. When the Ministry of Education investigated last time, only 30,000 yuan had been allocated. The city plans to establish 24 one-year short-term primary schools, with three classes per school, and 90 classes of short-term primary schools attached to ordinary primary schools in the 24th year. It will also promote six elementary schools, with a total of 13 grades, expand the grades of existing primary schools by 40 grades, and vigorously implement the two-part system, planning to establish 36 grades. In addition, it will improve private schools and try out mobile education to help promote free education.

Qingdao

Received a central subsidy of 41,000 yuan for free education and raised 53,000 yuan from the city. Education in the city has always been popular. All villages in rural areas have schools. The popularization method is to use existing school buildings and classes to implement the two-part system. Also, because each school has enough students and no spare rooms, it is possible for students in the two-part system to use each other, so a half-day two-part system is mostly adopted to facilitate management and education. In the whole urban area, a total of four ordinary classes were added, 24 two-part classes were converted, and six new two-part classes were added. In the rural area, the single-style編制 were all changed to two-part classes. In the rural area, 20 ordinary classes were added, 34 new two-part classes were added, and 154 one-part classes were converted. The above 24 ordinary classes, 40 newly added two-part classes, and 178 one-part classes were converted. In addition, new schools were established and classes were added or changed in the newly designated urban area. In fact, 311 classes can be added or changed in the 24th year, with an average of 40 children per class.

Nanjing

Received a central subsidy of 100,000 yuan for free education and raised 100,000 yuan from the city. 24 short-term primary schools with 221 classes and 11,019 students have been established. Short-term primary school classes were attached to 35 primary schools, public schools, and public education centers, with a total of 52 classes. There are 37 simplified primary schools in the urban area, with a total of more than 200 classes, and 56 simplified primary schools in the rural area, with a total of more than 160 classes.

Xikang

Received a central subsidy of 60,000 yuan for free education. In the first semester of the 24th year, seven ordinary primary schools and 40 annual short-term primary schools were established. The Ministry of Education has not yet received reports on the promotion of free education in the second semester.

Weihaiwei

Received a central subsidy of 8,000 yuan for free education and raised 7,250 yuan from local sources. There are 21,994 out-of-school children. The administrative region plans to establish 32 short-term primary schools, with a total of 64 classes, and promote grades, adopt a two-part system, and try out mobile education. Ministry of Education Supervisor Sun Guofeng Dies; Contracted Illness While Inspecting Guangdong; Died After Treatment in Beiping 159

(Nanjing, 18th) Sun Guofeng, a senior supervisor of the Ministry of Education, was dispatched to Guangdong at the beginning of the month to inspect education. Lei Zhen Talks About Education in Guangdong Province 160

(Nanjing, 28th) Lei Zhen arrived in Nanjing from Shanghai on the afternoon of the 28th. According to his talk, education in Guangdong Province has developed greatly in terms of quantity, but quality still needs to be improved. China Art Association: Art Exhibition Extended to October 2nd 164

The first art exhibition organized by the China Art Association has attracted more than 1,000 visitors every day since its opening.
