Other modern masters, such as Xie Gongzhan's chrysanthemums, Shi Chongpeng's green landscapes, and Wang Geshi's flowers, also added a lot of color to the venue. However, there were not many orders. The exhibition was originally scheduled for one week and would close at the end of the month. Now, in response to the requests of people from all walks of life, it has been extended for two more days and will close at 8 PM on the afternoon of October 2nd. Those who wish to visit should go as soon as possible.

"The Life of a Bank Employee" by Yang Yinpu Will Be Published Soon 169

"The Life of a Bank Employee" by Yang Yinpu contains twenty-one essays about the life of a bank employee. The arguments are insightful, and the writing style is light. It is the culmination of Mr. Yang's vernacular essays over the years. Among them, "The Ideal Bank Employee," "Air Conditioning in the Iron Cage," "The Psychology of Speculation," "Life's Unpayable Tuition Fees," "Extracurricular Studies," "The Troubles of Granting Loans," "The Price of a Cigarette," and "Final Accounting" all have unique insights, and the writing is also timeless and readable. The book is priced at six jiao, and reservations are only four jiao (plus one jiao and one fen for postage and registration). The reservation locations are the Life Bookstore and Liming Bookstore on Simalu in Shanghai. The deadline for reservations is October 15, and the publication date is October 16.

Detailed Explanation of Japanese Grammar 170

"Detailed Explanation of Japanese Grammar" by Wu Baojin focuses on literary language and extracts and explains colloquial language for comparison. The materials are extremely precise and rich. It is compiled from the excellent compilations of various literary grammar books. Each word has Chinese annotations, which is more convenient for Chinese people to learn by themselves. It is a total of more than 200,000 words. The end of the book also has ten appendices: (1) Idiomatic Formulas, (2) Latest Foreign Words, (3) Commonly Used Popular Words, (4) Article Analysis, (5) Various Slang and Colloquialisms, (6) Telegrams, (7) Letter Writing Methods and Formats, (8) Proposed Chinese Characters, Standard Characters, (9) Ministry of Education's Special Habitual Words, (10) Miscellany, etc. In addition, the difficulties for Japanese learners that must be understood and remembered are collected extensively and interpreted in detail, which is not available in other books. This is its greatest feature. The book is currently in print and has been prefaced by Xu Shiying, Ambassador to Japan, and proofread by Chen Wenlan, a Japanese language expert.

Yarn, Cotton, and Cloth Prices All See Increases 182

Osaka Telegraph, 28th: Futures prices for yarn have risen by 2.40 to 3.20 yuan, with the near month at 213 yuan and the far month at 205.60 yuan. Cotton futures prices have risen by 1.30 to 1.55 yuan, with the near month at 266.10 yuan and the far month at 65.35 yuan.

Piece Goods: Yarn and Thread Prices Rise Frequently; Cotton Cloth Becomes More and More Fierce in its Rise—Various Factories Still Find it Difficult to Meet Sales Demands—Yesterday, the cotton cloth market saw a dramatic rise in yarn and thread prices at the end of last week, and the cotton cloth market situation also became more and more fierce in its rise. Customer agents were even more enthusiastic in their purchases. Southern merchants showed the strongest interest. Guangdong merchants added huge amounts of white goods, including coarse white cloth, fine twill, and fine cloth. However, most transactions failed to materialize due to factories being out of stock. Only over 500 pieces of Ewo 11-pound Three Cats, Three Deer coarse cloth, and Shenxin 11-pound Siping Lotus coarse cloth were secured. More than 100 cases of serge and broadcloth were also transacted. Merchants from Yunnan and Fujian were also eager to purchase but were distressed by the lack of goods to supply. Merchants from Sichuan were also active, showing great interest in printed flannelette, Zhigong satin, serge, and colored twill. At the same time, northern merchants vigorously purchased绒布,钱呢, and serge. Merchants from the interior also continued to forge ahead, and the market situation became more and more prosperous. Selling prices rose uniformly, with printed flannelette seeing the most dramatic increase, rising by one cent per yard, which is calculated to be 4.5 jiao for each 45-yard piece. Broadcloth, serge, and Zhigong satin each rose by 1.5 to 3 jiao per piece, white flannelette rose by 1 to 2 jiao, coarse cloth with heavier weights were the most in demand, rising by 1 to 2 jiao per piece, while lighter weights rose by 5 fen. Coarse twill, fine cloth, and fine twill also rose by more than 1 jiao. For example, Shenxin factory products, including various grades of coarse cloth, fine cloth, fine twill, grey cloth, and坯布, have all increased by 2 jiao per piece, and it is said that the factory does not have the goods to supply.

Yellow Broadcloth Supply Cannot Meet Demand 183

The broadcloth market in general has been quite good recently. The market at the Guild is firm, and the number of people going to the Guild to certify and submit tax-paid certificates to the Customs is quite crowded. Both domestic and imported broadcloth are doing well, with yellow broadcloth having an even wider sales reach. Beijing and Hangzhou have both shown significant interest in purchasing, and the supply of Polish and domestic goods cannot meet demand. Zhanghua yellow broadcloth is therefore seizing the opportunity to increase prices by 1.5 jiao. Yesterday, domestic Zhanghua military uniform yellow broadcloth all rose to 2.60 yuan, Ewo to 2.65 yuan, Renli to 2.475 yuan, Polish goods (Huabo, Baoda, Baodali, Ruiyu, etc.) all sold for 2.60 yuan for first grade, 2.40 yuan for second grade, 1.90 yuan for third grade, and Yongfeng Unified brand for 2.35 yuan.

Securities: No Increase in Government Bond Deliveries for September; However, There Were Many Private Deliveries Outside the Market; The Market for the Whole Month Rose First and Then Fell 184

Yesterday (the 28th) was the date for the delivery of September futures at the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange. The total number of deliveries was 17,763,000 yuan. Of this amount, the clearing amount was 11,120,500 yuan. The amount delivered at the Exchange was only 6,422,500 yuan. The delivery quantity did not increase, but it was rumored that the number of private deliveries outside the market by various brokers was very large. In these troubled times, it is expected that spot goods would continue to flow out. The highest September futures prices were at the beginning of July 2-8, and the lowest was on September 24, the last day. The difference between the two was less than 4 yuan for the highest and less than 2 yuan for the lowest, and the stimulation from the environment became more and more intense. Initially, the market price rose sharply after the resolution in Guangdong. Subsequently, the issue in Guangxi eased the tension, and this cycle repeated itself. The market price hovered for a long period of time. After the peaceful resolution of the Guangxi issue, there were rumors of the Reorganization Public Bonds rising again, coupled with the serious smuggling in North China. Then the Chengdu incident occurred, followed by unfortunate accidents in Beihai and Hankou. Although there were no changes in the market, it ultimately lacked the strength to rise. After the Hong Kong incident occurred on September 23, which happened to be the last day of trading for September futures, people were shaken by this event. Large investors exited, and spot goods flowed out, and the market situation began to turn bearish. The clearing amounts and total transaction numbers are listed separately below (unit:

Silk and Tea: Only Ewo Has Some Silk Transactions 185

Yesterday in the overseas silk market, Yokohama rose slightly, New York was quiet, and Lyon was even more difficult to approach due to the passage of the French currency bill and the devaluation of the French franc. Ewo traded slightly in 3A grade and 83 uniformity 16.18 strands, and the price was relatively stable. There were only a few sales in the domestic silk market, and prices were slightly weak.

Precious Eyebrow and Pearl Tea Sales to Europe Become Active 186

Yesterday, the situation in the foreign firms' green tea market was quite lively. The sales of Precious Eyebrow and Pearl Tea from the Luzhuang and Shui roads to Europe suddenly became smooth. Concord, Ewo, Tongfu, Baochang, and other firms purchased a lot. The total transactions of green tea in the city reached more than 2,000 cases. The top-grade Precious Eyebrow from each of the Tunxi firms opened at 126 yuan, and the top-grade Pearl Tea from Pingshui opened at 62 yuan. However, the market prices of medium and low-grade goods still tended to fall due to the relatively large amount of inventory. The market situation still showed a rising and falling pattern. The large quantities of Qimen black tea purchased by the Jinlong Foreign Firm have all been priced, and there are also scattered transactions.

According to a report from the Tea Warehouses and Lai Guild, the green tea market last week had little development due to the holiday period in Morocco. However, various foreign firms sent out a considerable number of sales telegrams over the weekend. Yesterday, the market situation turned active. Ewo received a reply from the buyer and purchased 800 cases of Precious Eyebrow from various routes, with the prices being 46 yuan for Local Precious, 58 yuan for Anhui Precious, and 66 to 68 yuan for Tunxi Wuyuan Precious, and two batches of Pingshui Pearl Tea purchased before and after, totaling approximately 2,000 cases, at prices of 53 yuan to 54 jiao. Concord purchased 800 cases of Xiumei, with prices ranging from 18 to 23 yuan. There are also considerable negotiations on Pingshui Pearl Tea and Precious Eyebrow on the market, and there is hope for transactions in the coming days.

Sugar Market: Transactions of Five Rams Coarse White Sugar Increase; A Total of 1,582 Bags Were Sold 187

Yesterday, the sugar market was tighter due to news of the Ho Lan market closing. As a result, the Cantonese coarse white sugar auction sales were very smooth, and there was a shortage of supply. The Guild's clearing prices were 21.6 jiao for spot coarse granulated white sugar, up 1 jiao, and 6.5 yuan for re-export. Dongbai sugar also tightened, rising by 1 jiao to 5 fen, 21.4 jiao for spot No. 4, 6.5 yuan for re-export, 21.15 jiao for spot No. 8, 6.3 yuan for re-export, and 20.95 jiao for spot No. 9, 5.9 yuan for re-export. There were no changes in the local factory's cotton white sugar.

The Joint Company held its first auction of Cantonese sugar for this week yesterday. The total quota was 15,811 bags. The bidding price remained the same, and the interest from the firms suddenly increased, and the supply was insufficient for distribution. All the sugar was sold, including 5,913 bags of Shunde Factory's Five Rams coarse white sugar at 21.4 jiao, 4,250 bags of Shixin Factory's 父 at 21.2 jiao, and 3,425 bags of Quxi Factory's sugar at 21 yuan, and another 579 bags at 20.7 jiao, and another 1,644 bags of medium granulated white sugar at 19.3 jiao. Subsequently, prices increased, probably because Dutch coarse white sugar also showed signs of rebounding.

North-South Goods: Dried Fruits, Dates, Melon Seeds, Market Sentiment Firm 188

New Red Dates: Over the past two days, a total of over a thousand packages were opened, including more than seven hundred packages of Taizhou red dates, priced between eight and a half yuan to seven and a half yuan; over three hundred packages of chicken-heart red dates, priced between nine yuan and eight and a half yuan. The market for Yu Hong and Mian Hong dates remained stable.

New Walnuts: Recent arrivals, gradually drying, have seen prices rise. Currently, Shimen walnuts are priced at thirty yuan, Changping walnuts at twenty-six yuan, Taizhou walnuts at twenty and a half yuan in the south and eighteen and a half yuan, and Qingzhou walnuts at seventeen and a half yuan. Walnut meat: Customs goods are priced at thirty-six to thirty-seven yuan, Jinan goods at forty yuan, and Yancheng goods at thirty-one to thirty-two yuan.

Black Melon Seeds: With the increasing arrival of new Jiaozhou black melon seeds, prices remain firm. Yesterday, they opened at nineteen and a half yuan to nineteen yuan. Other varieties include Jikui seeds at twenty-four and a half yuan, Shuang Gou seeds at twenty-one yuan, Tushan seeds at twenty yuan and sixty cents, and Shuixikou seeds at twenty yuan.

Spring and Autumn

Snippets 189

— (Reclining Buddha)

Chinese people, after all, do not seek deep understanding and are content with the status quo. They fundamentally do not understand where Heaven is, what abilities Heaven possesses, and what relationship exists between Heaven and humanity. Yet, they regard Heaven as the master of destiny, the conductor of life, with sayings like "relying on Heaven for food," "Heaven's mandate is unchangeable," entrusting everything to Heaven, consigning everything to Heaven, attributing everything to Heaven. I truly do not understand why the Chinese people's belief in Heaven is so resolute?

In fact, even if we acknowledge the existence of Heaven, there is absolutely no such thing as a Heavenly mandate; what exists is only "Heavenly evolution." Without a Heavenly mandate, Heaven will never turn the poor and lowly into the rich and noble, nor the rich and noble into the poor and lowly. It will not doom the ambitious to fall, nor compel the complacent to advance. Only Heavenly evolution deserves considerable attention, because everything human is inescapable from the principles of Heavenly evolution. What are the principles of Heavenly evolution? They are survival of the fittest, the superiority of the strong and the elimination of the weak. Therefore, under natural evolution, you are only allowed to take the path of striving and advancing, and not allowed to be content with ease and comfort. Otherwise, you will undoubtedly be eliminated.

Therefore, relying on a Heavenly mandate is decadence for an individual, and relying on a Heavenly mandate is national ruin for a majority. Only by believing in Heavenly evolution can one be progressive and save the nation. Only a Heavenly mandate can destroy Heavenly evolution, while Heavenly evolution can restrain a Heavenly mandate.

Before us lie these two paths – a Heavenly mandate and Heavenly evolution. Should not everyone carefully consider their choice?

Biography of a Rotten-Haired Fellow 190

— 19

Those who live in or have visited Hangzhou must be very familiar with the term "Rotten-Haired Fellow." However, the Rotten-Haired Fellow described here is a "Decidedly Foreigner," whose extraordinary conduct merits a biography. "Rotten-Haired Fellow" is a transliteration of "Laumel." Generally, those who have been highly culturally invaded always forget their ancestors and regard foreign countries as being all-powerful. Thus, they simply "foreignize" even their own names to show their conversion to Westernization. Laumel is one such example, and his original Chinese name has been obscured as a result.

The Rotten-Haired Fellow was originally a country bumpkin from the interior. After receiving a Western baptism in a treaty port, he returned home in glory and immediately looked down upon the countryside as being backward, so he moved into the city. Although the city was hundreds of times better than the countryside, the Rotten-Haired Fellow still lamented not having a Western-style house to live in. Fortunately, at this time, he had not yet seen a flush toilet!

When the Rotten-Haired Fellow spoke, he often interspersed it with gibberish. This, rather than showing his erudition, was simply a habit. For example, if he was in a room and someone knocked on the door, he would not ask "Who is it?" but say "Goods"; instead of saying "Please come in," he would say "Keming." When he went to visit someone and inquired outside, he would not say "Hey," but would definitely say "Xia Luo." He liked to use gibberish in this way.

The Rotten-Haired Fellow once invested a large sum of money and traveled to the West for more than a year. Having eaten Western bread, he was naturally different from the common people. When someone invited him to be a director, after taking office, he lectured all his colleagues extensively about England and France. He also made it one of his major policy directions to have all the toilets uniformly renovated into flush toilets to enhance the appearance!

The Rotten-Haired Fellow treated his colleagues like a foreign master treats his servants, nitpicking and often scolding them. People all called him a "Decidedly Foreigner" (Sub-foreigner), because he could not utter three sentences without mentioning England or America.

Encomium: "What is the Rotten-Haired Fellow like? A minor foreigner, his skills stop here!"

Hu Die's Confession 191

— Manzi

After reading Hu Die's announcements in the Shen and Xin newspapers, I felt that she had recognized that the film industry must be 'committed to for life'. The day before yesterday, I obtained a complimentary ticket from a friend to see her starring in "Women's Rights" at the Jin Cheng Grand Theater. I wanted to understand whether her performance, after half a year away from the limelight, was improved or regressed. From beginning to end, I was not tired, even though it was past midnight and nearing dawn, the golden hour of slumber. This is because she performed in almost twenty out of the thirty-plus scenes of "Women's Rights", truly earning the title of lead actress. Moreover, transitioning between various roles such as a university student, a young woman, a bank clerk, a female teacher, and a female worker, each position should have different postures, emotions, and consciousness, fully embodied in every word and action, to create a distinction. In each change of position, she has different ways of stimulating her, and she should have different responses; and the result of different responses, but the same feeling, this kind of story, although not new, but the performance is very difficult. But she handled it very easily, after all, she is an experienced veteran.

The next day, my friend introduced me to the Star Film Company in Chulin Bridge, where she happened to be starring in "Eternal Smile". Indeed, she is the eternal smile, her amiability fully manifested in a dimple. On the filming set, she performs earnestly, even though the time is very long, due to the repeated "NGs" of the supporting actors, wasting a lot of time, and even the onlookers are somewhat anxious and bored, but after the "OK", she is still very happy to chat with us. She asked if I had seen "Women's Rights"? I said: I have seen it, she smiled and said, if you came to see our work during the production of "Women's Rights", I'm afraid you wouldn't have lasted five minutes, because it was the hottest part of summer, but we've gotten used to it.

As I was leaving her and walking out of the filming set, I said to my friend that I was convinced that Hu Die had recognized the greatness of film, and that she and Song Jiayu in Women's Rights, have the same ambition. Especially commendable is that she is in a more comfortable situation than Song Jiayu, and is absolutely unwilling to "stop the progress of her career for the sake of the union of the two sexes." We hope that "Women's Rights" is her confession.

Random Talks About Goldfish 192

— Wu Jiren

Mr. Xin Yu Tang Yan Yi (a mathematics professor at Jiaotong University, with a master's degree from the United States) has visited many times and does not disdain to associate with inferiors. Mr. Tang has recently become fond of ornamental fish. At his residence on Avenue Petain in West Shanghai, he has six sand tanks displaying various precious goldfish. Yesterday, he and his wife drove to Caohejing to specifically look for multicolored pearl goldfish and blue telescope goldfish. Mr. Tang has new business in Beiping, and entrusted someone to carry more than ten fine specimens on his return journey, all of which are rare in the south. Some of his friends also happily sought famous breeds from him, so he provided them nearby. Continuing to talk about the treatment of aquatic organisms, I was instructed on academic principles and benefited greatly. I was also told to recommend to audit a certain university. I lost my schooling at a young age and made mistakes when I grew up. In the way of fish, I have gained access to the door. I have received inquiries from all over the country from those who share the same hobby. I only want to study it again, but it is really difficult to answer fundamentally. At night, I feel guilty and ashamed. The sage said, "Learn after being troubled." Now that I can get this good opportunity, I should strive to improve and comfort the general expectations of teachers and friends.

Mr. Cai Dongjun, the director of the Shanghai Public Security Bureau, often pays unannounced visits to his jurisdiction in plain clothes. Three times last month he came to "Fish Swim Heaven". While admiring the fish, he inquired about the method of distinguishing male and female fish. I told him that the male fish looks at the fish's body, and the old fish touches the fish's abdomen. The greater the distance between the abdomen and the tail, the more masculine it is; the shorter it is, the more feminine it is. However, this method is sometimes not accurate, because the abdomen of male fish is also swollen. The method of touching is more appropriate. When picking up the fish, touch the fish's abdomen with your fingers. The female fish is soft, because the eggs are stored. (Although the eggs in the fish's abdomen are frequently scattered between spring and summer, they still cannot be completely scattered, so the difference between male and female is most obvious in spring and summer, and slightly worse in autumn and winter.) The scales of male fish are hard and not slightly different. Director Cai tried it by hand, laughed loudly and left. He once asked if he could prepare one or two red ones in the mansion to pass the leisure time after work. The answer was: This fish is too difficult to raise, and there is no such leisure. According to research, the female fish are more prosperous than the male, accounting for about six to four. I also asked Professor Tang. Tang said, this is the nature of the water, and it is difficult to answer without actually studying aquaculture. There is no shortage of experts in the country, and you should ask them. (Ji Ren's postscript: Guansheng's Fish Capital, I have resigned and left, and I am selling my own "Purple Micro Goldfish Factory". The address is also in Caohejing Town. Please send it to Yanling Jixia, Caohejing, if you are friendly.)

Rambling Talk

Private Ode to Paradise 193

— Qiu Chong

Prerequisites for Being an Immortal

The following passage, although similar to playful writing and slightly humorous, clearly reveals the truth and contains profound principles. For example, the mockery of Chunyu's son-in-law, the jesting of Dongfang's courtier, and the humorous insertions of Liu Ma Zi (Jing Ting) the comedian. The benevolent see benevolence, the wise see wisdom, each possessing satirical effects and far-reaching implications. The so-called laughing and scolding, arguing and advising, humorous words may even contain considerable sorrow and be filled with infinite grief, forged and organized by many bitter tears. It is not necessarily about sophistry to please, humor to delight, and must not be regarded as frivolous talk about romance, dental wit, just for giggles, without significance.

Previous people often compared Suzhou and Hangzhou to heaven. Now, Shanghai has surpassed them. The prosperity of the foreign concessions is simply hundreds of times that of Suzhou and Hangzhou. Roughly speaking, Shanghai can undoubtedly be called today's paradise. Since Shanghai is paradise, then we, the people living in paradise, needless to say, are all living gods, at the very least, no less than land immortals. Speaking of our living conditions in paradise, they are actually no less than those of gods. For example, immortals like to live in tall buildings, we have skyscrapers of twenty-odd floors to live in; gods can ride clouds and mist, traveling with the wind—we also have airplanes to sit on, gods have flowers that never fade in the four seasons and evergreens in the eight festivals—and we now have foreign varieties of rare flowers all year round, gods can transport fresh fruits from thousands of miles away and out of season—and we can now use airplanes and cold storage to do the same, and they come from across the ocean, even rarer and more valuable than theirs. Furthermore, the high-speed flight of trains and cars, isn't that the god's ability to shrink the ground? Wireless radio and photography, aren't those the gods' clairvoyance and keen hearing? Motorcycles and bicycles, aren't those the gods' Wind and Fire Wheels? Ships on the water and submarines under the water, aren't those water escape techniques? Walking at will in the basement, isn't that earth escape? (Although Shanghai does not yet have great projects such as underground trains like New York, it will definitely be possible to imitate them in the near future, which will be even more like earth escape,) the installation of central heating in cold weather and air conditioning in hot weather can change the climate, so the winter clothes and summer furs flaunted by the gods are not surprising at all! Moreover, the material civilization of Shanghai may even exceed that of heaven. Many speculative venues and novel games, I am afraid that the gods will shake their heads and stick out their tongues when they see them, ashamed that they have never experienced them! We actually roam here like immortals, what else is there to be unsatisfied with? However, dare I ask: To what extent is our life as gods in this paradise truly happy? And why do most immortals feel deeply distressed, bored, and complain? Could it be because people are too insatiable, like a beggar wanting to be an emperor, and wanting to be a beggar again after becoming an emperor?

It must be known that there are several grades and types of immortals, and immortals are not necessarily happy! Liu Hai scattering money, Lu Dongbin turning stones into gold, making money in the right way, with daily income, economically well-off, and living comfortably, these friends in the capitalist class, even if they don't become immortals, are still very happy. As for those laborers, such as the Cowherd and the Weaver Girl, owing the Heavenly Emperor's betrothal money, anxious day and night, plowing and weaving, just busy repaying debts, and also forcibly separating the couple, only able to cross the magpie bridge to meet once a year, that kind of immortal situation, I am afraid, is not very good? Especially we who have read a few dead books, relying solely on writing to maintain a living, and are called poor scholars by the masses, only getting a meager amount of alfalfa rations and absolutely not沾染ing any golden or silver aura, what fun is there in becoming an immortal in this kind of hard and bitter life! What's more, this paradise of Shanghai is especially built on money, and we who are listed as immortals are ultimately earth immortals and half-immortals with shallow Taoism, and have not learned the practical skills of immortal transcendence, so naturally we should suffer more! Please see: gods can wear "ivy as clothes" and "lotus leaves as skirts", can we? Gods can eat wind and drink dew, whistling in mist and haze, or take white stones as bait, and the essence of the sun and moon as food, and can even eat iron pellets when embarrassed, and drink copper juice when thirsty, can we? Gods can also make the sky their curtain and the earth their seat, pillow on streams and live in caves, sleep against the clouds, and sleep near the latrine, can we? Regarding the three major issues of clothing, food and housing, gods can solve them without spending a penny, which will inevitably become a fatal injury and a piercing pain for us; in addition, the living standards in paradise are particularly high compared to the mortal world, and it is difficult to move an inch without money, and we poor immortals who fill the ranks and have no skills happen to lack money the most, so the fairyland is desolate, the expression is embarrassed, and we feel more sad than all the sentient beings in the human world! From this, we can draw the following conclusion: Shanghai is indeed worthy of being paradise, and we can also be immortals, but the only prerequisite is to fully raise a sum of money before we can live peacefully in the fairyland and receive fragrant flower offerings, otherwise, even if we are omnipotent Great Luo True Immortals, we will only have to sigh at the roof and be at a loss, unless we quickly borrow a finger from Mr. Lu Dongbin! Therefore, the true happy immortals are only limited to rich and noble immortals, otherwise, since they have become immortals, why bother to learn the ability to turn stones into gold?

No wonder recently many immortals are infatuated with the prosperity of paradise, yearning for the happiness of immortals, and yet feeling cold to the bone, lacking the capital to become immortals, with fire in their eyes and ice in their bodies, everything is desirable but not attainable, so their appetite is greatly aroused and their desires are high, and they no longer care about the Qing rules that immortals should abide by, becoming extremely evil and ugly, desperately jumping around, even if they violate the rules and ruin their reputation, they will not hesitate. I therefore think that the phrase "immortal jump" circulating in Shanghai's population is probably derived from this? Hehe!

However, I have to say it again: It is also not easy to be an immortal in paradise. If there is too much money, I am afraid that fierce gods and evil spirits such as "Bi Ma Wen", "Marshal Wen", and "Bull Demon King" will have evil intentions when they see the wealth, and use violence to rob or kidnap, living in fear all day long, as if in prison, and dare not cross the thunder pool easily. Isn't that still very unhappy? Fortunately, Liu Hai and Lu Dongbin's money comes very easily, so it's okay to give up a small portion of the charitable wealth and hire a few fully armed Wei Bodhisattvas and tall and mighty Four Heavenly Kings to protect them and carefully guard the door. Not only can it enhance the spectacle and increase the momentum, but also the security is meticulous and the security is strict, what else to worry about evil stars and fierce Tai Sui coming to "kidnap the God of Wealth"!

Shen Bao Medical Supplement

General Talk on Pulmonary Tuberculosis 195

— Li Zhao Zhang

(Lecture at St. Mary's Girls' School)

The Pathological State of Chinese People

On the road, in public places, hunchbacked, stooped, listless, weak, no one will deny that these are Chinese people. Why are Chinese people so decadent, and why is the Chinese nation so weak? This is a very serious question. Foreigners look down on us Chinese the most. Even the Indians who have already lost their country don't think much of us. They say that China is a sick country, and almost everyone in China has problems. This is such a painful thing.

The Situation of Tuberculosis in China

There are many reasons for the decline of the Chinese nation, among which tuberculosis is one of the biggest reasons. According to experts, one in every twenty-five people in China has tuberculosis, and four thousand out of every 100,000 people have tuberculosis. There are 16 million people with tuberculosis in the country, and 1.6 million people die from tuberculosis every year. On average, twenty-five people die from tuberculosis every ten minutes. This mortality rate is unparalleled in the world. Experts have also statistically found that there are 140,000 people with tuberculosis in Shanghai. Just imagine that so many people with tuberculosis are spreading and spreading every day. I am afraid that in less than two years, we will all become victims.

Stamps Transmit Tuberculosis

Recently, an American magazine contained that most of the staff in the US post office have developed tuberculosis. The news spread and shocked the entire United States. After research by experts, it was found that this disease is completely transmitted by stamps, because most people use sputum to stick stamps, and inevitably there are people with tuberculosis. After the stamps are dry, the tuberculosis bacteria spread. Because there are many letters in the post office, and they breathe the air full of tuberculosis bacteria all day long, they get infected. Tuberculosis is everywhere, which is terrible.

Tigers Killed by Tuberculosis

In the spring of this year, the tiger in the Nanshi Zoo suddenly died. All parties were very surprised. After an autopsy by the Health Bureau, it was found that the tiger had third-stage tuberculosis and died of incurable disease. The reason why the tiger suffered from tuberculosis was because it ate the sputum of tuberculous tourists. Look, the tiger can't defeat tuberculosis. Tuberculosis is also fiercer than a tiger. This problem is really too serious.

The Source and Transmission of Tuberculosis

Lack of sleep, unclean diet, dirty housing, lack of exercise, depression, and lack of hygiene habits are all the main causes of tuberculosis. Living, eating, using utensils, and close conversation with patients are all ways of transmitting tuberculosis.

Spitting is Like Throwing a Bomb

The worst habit of Chinese people is spitting everywhere. Because this is a serious problem, the Anti-Tuberculosis Association holds a week of campaigns to stop spitting every year, and has invited doctors to take sputum for testing in the Nanjing Road area. It was found that 30% of them had tuberculosis bacteria. Machine gun bullets can kill people, but spitting everywhere is not the same as throwing machine gun bullets everywhere? In the same way, it can kill people and kill us.

Prevention and Treatment of Tuberculosis

Regular daily exercise and work, sufficient sleep, cleanliness of diet and housing, a happy mood, and isolation and separate meals from patients are all methods of preventing tuberculosis. But unfortunately, when we feel that our appetite is poor, night sweats, coughing up blood, the facts tell us that tuberculosis has already come. However, Chinese people are born with superstitious ideas. When they are sick, they only know how to pray to gods and recite Buddha, but they don't know that praying to gods and reciting Buddha will not only not improve the patient, but will make them heavier every day. Hundreds of thousands of Chinese people die unjustly every year in this way. Therefore, once we find the above symptoms, we should go to the hospital immediately, or ask a doctor to diagnose and treat us. But the most important thing is prevention, because it is dangerous to wait until you are sick before seeking treatment.

Hope Everyone Cooperates to Prevent Tuberculosis

Foreigners often bully us, mainly because we lack the power of unity. We only shrink back and are lazy when things happen. You can see that most people on the road put their hands in their sleeves and tie up their sleeves. This fully shows that our nation only stands by when things happen, and only hesitates when encountering difficulties. We should improve this bad habit. We, regardless of men and women, should join hands, not talk empty words, not sing high-sounding tunes, and hope that everyone has the spirit of a 'tumbler' and the courage and sacrifice of President Sun to revive our declining Chinese nation.

My Humble Opinion on Promoting New Medical and Health in Rural Areas 196

— Han Zhongying

To revive the countryside, although it requires efforts in all aspects, running rural medical and health care is also an urgent task for the current rural medical and health care: it is indeed a fact recognized by modern health experts, politicians, and important people in society. Because our country is based on agriculture, farmers account for more than 85% of the national population, and rural areas account for more than 90% of the national territory, so in the past, many people said: 'The rural problem is the whole problem of China'; I can also say now; 'The rural medical and health problem is also the whole Chinese medical and health problem'; then, according to the above two points, the importance of rural medical and health care, the relationship between farmers and the country can be seen.

Speaking of the history of rural medical and health care in our country, it is very naive. However, in the past seven or eight years, when public health has been extended to rural areas: a new medical term has been produced, which is the germination period when new medical and health care is promoted to rural areas.

Because farmers live in remote rural areas, new education is difficult to popularize, and most farmers have not received new knowledge and new education. This has created a stubborn brain, and the remaining poison of superstition is deeply rooted in the brain. Once they get sick, they don't know how to seek medical treatment, and there is no scientific new medicine to seek. They don't know how to take care of themselves during illness, and how to deal with it after illness. They completely rely on their long-trained copper muscles and iron bones to resist the disease and fight against the disease demon. If they are not strong enough, when they can't resist and can't fight the disease demon, the power of the bacteria will be greatly expanded, and the disease will worsen. Then the whole family will panic, anxiously holding a full of grief and ghost fetus, waiting for the coming of the god of death. They always think that they have offended the sky, or stopped the god's arrow. So they seek gods and worship Buddha, burn incense and ask for divination. If they are usually strong, or the disease they suffer from is lighter, they will heal once, which is the Buddha's power, the god's grace, and the Bodhisattva's諭. If the disease worsens or even dies, they always say; 'It is destined by heaven, and the fate should be so'; or say; 'Yan Wang呌s him or her death will not be wrong'! As long as you step into the countryside and encounter these things, you will hear these kinds of words. They don't know: the disease is caused by bacteria (microorganisms that can cause disease), and is caused by unhygienic conditions. Under this situation, how many wronged ghosts have been added to the underworld? As a result, the mortality rate has increased, the expenditure on medical expenses, and the decline of business, the reduction of economic productivity, and the creation of a collapsed and irreparable rural area.

Then, the only wonderful way to save the country and survive now: promoting new medical and health care in rural areas is the supreme strategy; the development of new medical and health care undertakings can reduce the mortality rate of diseases, and can promote people's health, prolong people's lives, increase the ability to work and economic productivity, and the improvement of the country's status in the international community is a fact that cannot be denied by ordinary people.

Indeed, new medical and health care has made considerable progress and remarkable achievements in recent years. However, it is often seen or heard that the difficulties encountered by the pioneers of rural medical and health care and the repeated failures have caused a psychological embarrassment to those who have not served in rural areas. Therefore, the author's knowledge is shallow and the writing is rough. Without hesitation, there are the following points, which are published in this newspaper's medical supplement for the reference of comrades who intend to run rural medical and health care: have a definite goal and a preventive plan to jointly seek the progress of rural medical and health care promotion. Regarding Li Kejia and the Illness of Li Kejia (1) 197

— Chen Duanbai

(I) Introduction

The term "Li Kejia" is relatively new and perhaps worth introducing. In the ranks of various infectious disease pathogens, it is a rather late newcomer, originating just twenty years ago, during a time when bacteriology was in decline. Therefore, it holds even more significance for introduction.

Li Kejia is undoubtedly a pathogen. However, within the field of bacteriology, due to its unique and distinct characteristics, it is difficult to categorize it into any existing bacterial system. Therefore, those who identified it as a pathogen, for the sake of temporary classification and to honor the two scholars who sacrificed themselves in initially discovering it, named the genus of this pathogen after the surname of the first scholar, calling it Rickettsia. This was combined with the surname of the second sacrifice, naming it Rickettsia prowaxeki, the pathogen of epidemic typhus, which also serves as a model representative of the Rickettsia genus, Types spezies (Typus).

(II) History

Following the outbreak of the European War, epidemic typhus also raged. At that time, many scholars dedicated themselves to exploring the pathogen. After numerous discoveries, one by one they were refuted. Eventually, the first, Ricketts, (possibly Polish! A stateless person at the time)

whose name will perish with the end of human civilization, proving him more noble than so-called national heroes limited to one era. He was a great hero who sacrificed himself in the struggle for human survival against nature. His death was truly heavier than Mount Tai. In 1910, he discovered small bodies (microorganisms) within the tissues of animals infected with epidemic typhus, now known as Li Kejia. Prowazek, based on his life status, was convinced that it was a pathogen and published his research on Mexican typhus (Tabardillo). Not long after, this promising young scholar was infected and succumbed to Li Kejia. He died aspiring to his goal. However, others followed in his footsteps. Prowazek continued Ricketts' research and published his report on the discovery of this pathogen in 1913. However, not long after, he also followed in Ricketts' footsteps and died of epidemic typhus. Rocha Lima continued the work, proving the reproduction of these small bodies in the epithelial cells of the intestinal wall of lice, the vectors of epidemic typhus. From a biological and morphological point of view, they were identical to those discovered by Ricketts and Prowazek. He published in 1916, confirming that these small bodies, which resembled bacteria, were indeed the pathogens of epidemic typhus, based on pathogenicity, biological state, and morphology. Since then, researchers have followed this path to seek similar pathogens in similar diseases, and successful findings have continued to be published. Today, we know that several diseases, previously with unknown pathogens, are caused by Li Kejia, for example,

Rocky Mountain spotted fever Rockv muuntain spot ted fever

Trench fever Febris quintana Wojbynicn

Mexican typhus Taqardillo Brill Diseaso

Manchurian typhus Ma nchau Fleckfider

Common Knowledge Q&A about Diseases 198

— Cheng Hanzhang

(92) Gout (Middle)

If gout becomes chronic, what symptoms appear? Chronic gout causes symptoms such as swollen and deformed joints, tophi, and Heberden's nodes.

What does joint swelling and deformation look like?

The small joints of the patient's fingers and toes show persistent changes, especially in the fingers. Nodular or spindle-shaped thickening occurs at the metacarpophalangeal joints, curving towards the ulnar side.

What are tophi? Tophi are uric acid salt deposits in various parts of the body, most commonly in the auricle and fingers. They are white, pea-sized nodules. They can also occur in the olecranon process, or in the bursae above the knee joint on the extensor side of the elbow. If these masses are punctured with a needle, uric acid and what are called Heberden's nodes will be found.

Heberden's nodes are localized bony thickenings at the distal interphalangeal joints of the second and third fingers or toes. They are also unique to gout patients.

What diseases are concurrent with gout?

Uric acid stones, diabetes, hyperlipidemia, and arteriosclerosis often occur.

Investigation Report on the Health Conditions of Xiaoshi, Zhejiang (2) 199

— Shen Songnian

(VI) Shops and Public Places

The entire town of Xiaoshi only has three pawnshops for civilians (originally there were four, but due to the impact of the rural collapse, one closed down this year, and the remaining three are also struggling), eight money shops, only four of which are still open. The Bank of China occupies the highest authority in the town's financial sector. There are three bookstores, two printing shops, and no fewer than two thousand four hundred other businesses, half of which have capital exceeding ten thousand yuan. However, due to the surge in the economic recession, the town is close to the collapsing countryside, and commerce is declining more rapidly. All industries are already at the end of their rope, especially small businesses. Only the rice industry is doing well, not diminishing despite the decline of other markets. This year, the number of rural goods stores has increased slightly, reaching over thirty. Originally, the market in Xiaoshi was very prosperous, once known as "Little Shanghai." Since the silk and tea industries plummeted, the town, which thrived on three industries, now relies only on the rice industry to barely survive.

There are about ten hotels in the entire town. The First Hotel on Ganhe Street has relatively complete facilities and pays attention to hygiene and cleanliness. The others either lack light or are unhygienic, truly a manifestation of the town's immature understanding of hygiene. Only three restaurants remain open. There are many dim sum shops, the most famous being Jiang Shunxing, which has two locations in the north and south markets. The most famous tea and pastry shops are Tian Yixing and Chen Xinyuan, whose shortbread and mooncakes are renowned. There is also a Shaoxing branch tea and pastry shop, whose Shaoxing cakes and pastries are quite popular with the locals, so business is still thriving. There are three large-scale teahouses, the most hygienic being Dafugui, which has good light and air and relatively complete facilities. The others, numbering no fewer than two hundred, mostly have insufficient air and are unhygienic. The famous old "Yiyuan" is where the local gentry drink tea, and the gentry of Xiaoshi go there every day. "Tongfuyuan" is a rest area for the education community, and "Ruyige" is a gathering place for opium addicts. There is only one bathhouse in the entire town, and business is not thriving. The sanitary facilities are excellent, but it has been losing money for years and is about to be unsustainable, a reflection of the people of Xiaodi's lack of attention to bathing, which is a manifestation of immature hygiene knowledge. Even wealthy families do not have special bathhouses, let alone others?

The streets in the town are not wide. People used to only use two-person sedan chairs, but now there are bicycles and rickshaws that have just started to be trialed. Bicycles are only used for recreation. The post office started using bicycles to deliver express mail in mid-June.

Medicinal Plants of Domestic Origin (Continued) 200

— Zhou Mengbai

7. Jingjie (Schizonepeta) Nepeta japenica, Maxim

"Plant" originally from China, can be cultivated in gardens, an annual herb. Stems up to sixty centimeters high, the whole plant covered with short hairs. Leaves petiolate, pinnately divided, lobes linear or lanceolate, entire margin, obtuse. Verticillasters terminal, flowering in early summer with pale red small calyx-shaped flowers. The whole plant is aromatic.

Do not confuse with Chenopodium ambrosioides, L. of the Quinoa family.

"Crude drug" Jingjie (False Perilla) Herba Nepetae 1.8, is collected from its flower spikes and stems and leaves and dried. Commercially available products are usually about three to five millimeters long, finely chopped, green, with a unique aroma.

"Ingredients" The whole herb yields 1.8% of essential oil. The main components of the essential oil are d-Menthene and non-optically active Menthone, and also contains d-Limonene.

"Medicinal use" Old saying: Jingjie is a diaphoretic and wind-expelling medicine, and also an essential medicine for treating boils and for pre- and postpartum. A single dose is eight centimeters, made into a decoction.

Example prescription: Jingjie Decoction, effective for treating nosebleeds and other bleeding conditions. Jingjie (8.0) 100, make a decoction for one person and take it all at once. Gui Jing Decoction, for treating coma, back stiffness, and postpartum convulsions. Angelica, Jingjie

The above two flavors are decocted with wine or water and taken. Wind-expelling and detoxifying decoction, for treating swelling and pain.

Jingjie, Fangfeng, Du Huo, Licorice, Forsythia, Burdock seeds, the above six flavors, made into a decoction.

Daily Fee of Three Cents for Hospitalization and Convalescence (Continued) 201

— Ding Huikang

The Success of National Medical and Pharmaceutical Control How is the Health Protection of the Chinese People?

Other cities that have successfully implemented this project include Rochester, Dallas, Houston, Los Angeles, Roseville, Memphis, Minneapolis, St. Paul, Newark, Norfolk, Oklahoma, San Antonio, San Francisco, and Washington, D.C.

In North Carolina and Alabama, large-scale provincial insurance programs are underway, and similar programs will be established in Boston and other cities by the end of this year. However, membership is limited to groups and requires a minimum of ten people joining simultaneously. Furthermore, only employed individuals are eligible to join at the time of enrollment.

The New York Hospital Service Insurance Company is currently only willing to accept fifty new members per week.

A 57-year-old man in New York strongly opposed joining when he was first encouraged to do so. However, three weeks after joining, he was admitted to the hospital with severe pneumonia. Upon recovering and being discharged, the hospital bill was only $2.60. Another unemployed member suffered a severe fall and was admitted to the hospital. After X-ray and medication treatment, he was discharged after a week of hospitalization, without paying a penny. Thank-you letters from other members who received free medical treatment due to illness have piled up like mountains.

According to Huikang, despite the development of sports and the progress of public health among the American people, the annual medical expenses amount to 3.6 billion yuan, averaging 30 yuan per person. The cost of medical care is not considered low, but the people benefit from medical security and improved national health, which contributes greatly to various social construction projects. The nation's productivity also increases as a result, and its prosperity is by no means accidental. Furthermore, it can be said that all progress in society and the nation is based on the development of medicine, which is not merely a passive charitable cause, but a noble construction project and a necessity for the masses. I traveled to Europe several years ago and was filled with admiration and envy at the development of medical affairs and the improvement of national health in various countries. The fundamental reason is the success of medical control and adjustment methods. For example, Germany already has 20 million people enrolled in health insurance. If each person pays 5 marks per month, that amounts to 1.2 billion marks per year for medical and construction expenses. According to the 1930 statistics of the United States, the total annual medical expenses reached 3.6 billion yuan, averaging 30 yuan per person per year. From this, it can be seen that medicine is an economic construction, gathering the economic strength of the masses to protect their health and promote the construction of medical affairs, and its control and adjustment center, namely disease insurance agencies, or health and health insurance agencies.

Talking Points

Abyssinia's Representative Allowed to Continue Attending 202

— I

According to a recent Geneva dispatch, the Credentials Committee of the League of Nations has decided that the Abyssinian delegation may continue to attend and enjoy the rights of a member state. Therefore, it is generally believed that Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations is likely unavoidable. When the Abyssinian representative went to Geneva to attend the League of Nations meeting, the League of Nations felt extremely difficult to deal with this matter, and it was quite difficult to please both sides. Now the Credentials Committee of the League of Nations has decided that the Abyssinian delegation can continue to attend, which is not only a relief for Abyssinia, but also a relief for the League of Nations. This is one of the most satisfactory things the League of Nations has done recently.

Suppose the League of Nations does not allow the Abyssinian delegation to attend this time, where will the prestige of the League of Nations be? And the opening of the League of Nations conference is equivalent to not opening, because the League of Nations has not already resolved that Italy is an aggressor? Hasn't the League of Nations already implemented economic sanctions against Italy? Hasn't the League of Nations already denied the occupation of other countries' territories by force? Now the League of Nations has hardly cancelled the economic sanctions against Italy, but the resolution that Italy is an aggressor and denies the occupation of other countries' territories by force has not been revoked, then although Abyssinia is in fact equal to being lost, the name of Abyssinia still exists, on what basis should the League of Nations not allow the Abyssinian delegation to attend?

Suppose the League of Nations allows the Abyssinian delegation to attend this time, Italy will definitely express extreme anger, which is also expected by the League of Nations, isn't it? But why is the League of Nations able to uphold justice, be willing to offend Italy, which is powerful and has great power, and assist Abyssinia, which exists in name but not in reality? I think there must be some reasons for this. The first is that if the League of Nations considers Italy's withdrawal from the League of Nations this time and does not allow the Abyssinian representative to attend, not only will the face of the League of Nations be lost, but Italy, which swallows up the clouds and dreams, will not put the League of Nations in its eyes, and it will be even more difficult to deal with Italy in the future. It is better to save some face and resolutely decide that the Abyssinian delegation can continue to attend the League of Nations, this is the first meaning.

It is heard that the committee has convened several meetings, and in addition to the above decision, it has also resolved that the legality of the Abyssinian delegation's credentials shall not be requested to be determined by the International Court of Justice in The Hague, because the Abyssinian representative has already been allowed to attend the conference temporarily, which is enough to make the problem more complicated. In addition, the Abyssinian delegation cannot but make reservations on certain reasons stated in the report of the Credentials Examination Committee, because these reasons are in fact in conflict with the principle of non-recognition of occupation of land by force. If we look at these two points, the League of Nations' decision to allow the Abyssinian representative to attend the conference is still a tactic, one is to "attend the conference temporarily," and the other is that certain reasons stated conflict with the principle of non-recognition of occupation of land by force. What kind of reasons are the so-called certain reasons? It is difficult to know, but since it conflicts with the principle of occupation of land by force, then certain reasons are not very beneficial to Abyssinia, which can also be imagined. Judging from these two points, Abyssinia's attending representative is only temporary, so Mussolini in Italy calmly deals with the environment without immediately withdrawing from the League of Nations, which also makes sense.

Old Friend 205

— Liang Qijun

Chen Yishi, a waiter at the ×× Hotel, lived in a building with his companion Yang Tianhua. Chen Yishi was a lean man in his late twenties. Life had etched not-so-deep scars on his dark, swarthy, Southern-tinged, stubborn triangular face. His upper and lower limbs revealed a mismatch that was very difficult to

Page 20

please— a deformed development that made his lower limbs stronger than his upper limbs. When he walked, he often reminded one of a long-legged rooster walking.

In late September in Jiangnan, early autumn had already soothed people with a cool, soft breeze. But he was still wearing that thin white uniform. This was our second meeting. In our first meeting, we lightly skimmed over casual conversation.

He and I had once worked together in a Portuguese (we mostly called the Portuguese "salty shrimp props") Western restaurant in Hong Kong. I remembered that whenever he ran out of money, an interesting impression would appear before my eyes—

"Jesus loves me, I love—" He opened his hands, seeming to feel that everything was hopeless, and then, he raised his head and sang.

"Alas, Father in Heaven—" What followed was complaining about his own extravagance and regretting that his hard-earned money had been wasted on improper uses.

"Come to my place to hang out," he said haltingly, while pulling down the bottom of his uniform with both hands.

We walked silently along North Sichuan Road for a long stretch. In late mid-September, we had an unforgettable and painful day, but people had forgotten. "Mooncakes" displayed in the windows of food stores easily attracted the attention of some pedestrians.

"Maybe celebrating the Mid-Autumn Festival will alleviate a little of our nation's sorrow," I couldn't think of appropriate words to express my feelings. I spoke so clumsily, so ineptly.

"A consumptive ghost singing drum lyrics—" He glared at me, his lips slightly moving. The next sentence, "Making merry when death is imminent," seemed to be tacitly understood.

I was bewildered. Every time I walked along North Sichuan Road, my heart would sink. Because I couldn't fully know to which owner the space of this so-called "Mysterious Street" belonged.

Turning into a narrow alley off East Wuchang Road, another world seemed to unfold here— the air was foul: the stench of urine and feces and the sickening atmosphere evaporating from piles of garbage permeated every corner or drain. The various enticing shouts of the peddlers, mixed with the clamorous noises of uneducated women and children. There was also a small school that had evolved from a private school, from which a burst of singing was heard from time to time. A hoarse voice, outstanding and surpassing all others, shouted very shrilly and very clearly: "Arise! Ye who refuse to be slaves!"

Chen Yishi's residence was behind that school, in a dark room with poor light. First, he introduced me to his roommate, and I shifted my gaze to the face of the newly acquainted.

"This is Mr. Yang Tianhua."

He gestured towards me with his right hand.

We nodded to each other. I examined his well-proportioned body and a face that was not unpleasant. Then, I turned to Chen Yishi,

"How has life been?"

"Us, what is there to talk about?" Chen Yishi said faintly.

"We are living day by day in the dungeon," Yang Tianhua blurted out.

"Alas, Father in Heaven—" Chen Yishi started singing listlessly, in a tone like singing "Xipi" (a type of Cantonese opera).

"Father in Heaven, screw your Father in Heaven."

Yang Tianhua cursed in annoyance.

I didn't understand why my old friend hadn't changed his bad temper. It was a very embarrassing habit.

Chen Yishi recounted his life after our separation. He pulled down the bottom of his uniform with his hands, speaking. He spoke very slowly, as if with great effort. Obviously, he was gathering all abstract words to avoid recounting the misfortunes of reality.

"Ah Yang is right, we are living day by day in the dungeon…"

However, he neglected to mention the reasons for all the economic downturns, only sighing as if with a sense of it all:

"Fate is not as good as others, so one is naturally inferior."

That was wrong. I never agreed with their claim. What I regretted most was that they entrusted the power to control the ups and downs of life to "fate." In fact, our society has a close relationship with life. Internal and external troubles have caused society to fall into a quagmire of unease, and indirectly affected our lives, so it presents a dim grayness.

We continued talking for a long time. Finally, Chen Yishi concluded:

"In the final analysis, life is built on money. We lack money, so our lives are withered and painful."

What surprised me was that this time Yang Tianhua also sympathized with Chen Yishi's words, "What is most difficult for us to solve is the problem of money, yes, money!…" Yang Tianhua seemed to think that his roommate's theory was very adequate, and a look of triumph flowed between his eyebrows when he spoke.

"If someone gave you money and taught you to be a traitor, would you go?"

I couldn't think of any more ruthless and straightforward words to persuade them.

Trivial Notes from a Fishing Village (Continued) 206

— Yun Hai

The people passed the fifth day in extreme anxiety.

Every day, this group waited from sunrise until the sun gave them an insulting sneer and then slipped away behind the western hills, always treading the seashore with uneasy minds. As they gazed at the vast expanse of the sea, at those places they knew so well, when they were lost in thought, they couldn't help but be reminded by one of their companions:

"Why isn't there any news yet?"

Then, the old wrinkles on their foreheads would furrow, and they would walk a few steps with worry and fatigue.

Their brows knitted tightly, each heart calculating that news, that news that was like a life-or-death verdict—either struggling against the waves, or, more unfortunately, lingering at home waiting to die. For a moment, they thought of that glimmer of hope: anyway, taking away one or two from among seven or eight, maybe fate wouldn't touch them; however—

"It should be our turn, so why is it still silent?"

That was still watching the sky: watching the changing clouds in the sky to get through the days, letting hunger devour them.

This day, the weather was not good, and a black cloud drifted from afar. The entire sky seemed to be pressed down as heavy as lead, and the people were squeezed as if they were about to explode. On this side, five people were sitting watching the sky, but Old Five was walking back and forth angrily, having just severed everyone's emotions in a dissatisfactory conversation. Therefore, the post seemed particularly dull and unbearably uncomfortable.

After a while, Old Three jumped up violently, hopping madly:

"I can't take it anymore, I can't take it anymore! Even if you want me to stop watching the water, you have to give me a message earlier so that people can think of a way out. Damn it, that old tortoise, eating ash old man!"

"Even if you stop, as long as there are boats, you won't starve to death like this even if you set up a ferry in the provincial capital! Damn it, rely on you?"

This young and strong lad even spat heavily on the ground. Eighth Brother, this particularly casual fellow, his casual nature, was even more infuriating.

"There's still no despair, why is everyone in such a hurry? Third Brother, it's not you I'm afraid of, it's me...!"

You!

Old Three didn't care about anything and punched Eighth Brother on the forehead. Thus, the people passed this day in吵嚷.

The next day, people were still so muddled, either this family beating his wife, or that family taking it out on the children. People were anxiously waiting for the news, but there wasn't even a shadow of it.

In the evening, a surprising piece of news finally pricked everyone awake. The news, Old Three knew it earliest, according to him, was: Boat boss Li Laofu's father hanged himself at home.

Sun Yu's Three Masterpieces 213
